śrīdharadāsasaṅkalitama.rā. = anargharāghavaamaru = amaruśatakaḥu.nī. = ujjvalanīlamaṇiu.rā.ca. = uttararāmacaritada.rū. = daśarūpakamdhva. = dhvanyālokaḥpadyā. = padyāvalīpra.ca. = prabodhacandrodayambā.rā. = bālarāmāyaṇaḥbh.ra.si. = bhaktirasāmṛtasindhumā.a.mi. = mālavikāgnimitrammā.mā. = mālatīmādhavaḥvi.śā.bha. = viddhaśālabhañjikāśā.pa. = śārṅgadharapaddhatiśṛ.ti. = śṛṅgāratilakamsa.u.ka. = saduktikarṇāmṛtamsa.ka.ā. = sarasvatīkaṇṭhābharaṇamsā.da. = sāhityadarpaṇamsu.ā. = subhāṣitāvalīsu.ra. = subhāṣitaratnākarasu.ra.bhā. = subhāṣitaratnabhāṇḍāgāramsū.mu. = sūktimuktāvalisaduktikarṇāmṛtamśrīdharadāsasaṅkalitammaṅgalamprajñāṃ kāmapi sampadaṃ ca kurute yatpādasaṃvāhanaṃnityaṃ śāmyati viṣvagandhatamasaṃ yaccakṣurunmīlanāta|yatpādārghyapayo vidhūya duritaṃ niḥśreyasaṃ yacchatisvānte naḥ sa vasatvanāratamanākhyeyasvarūpo hariḥ ||1||prastāvaḥśauryāṇīva tapāṃsi bibhrati bhayaṃ yasminna yasyāvadhirjñāne dāna iva dviṣāmiva jayo yenendriyāṇāṃ kṛtaḥ |samrājāmiva yogināmapi gururyaśca kṣamāmaṇḍalesa śrīlalakṣmaṇasena ekanṛpatirmuktaśca jīvannabhūta||1||tasyāsītpratirājatadvṛtamahāsāmantacūḍāmaṇirnāmnā śrībaṭudāsa ityanupamapremaikapātraṃ sakhā |tāpaṃ santamasaṃ harannaharahaḥ kīrtiṃ dadhatkaumudīṃsākṣādakṣayasūnṛtāmṛtamayaḥ pūrṇaḥ kalānāṃ nidhiḥ ||2||śrīmānśrīdharadāsa ityadhiguṇādhāraḥ sa tasmādabhūdākaumārapārapauruṣaparādhīnasya yasyāniśam |lakṣmīrvedavidāṃ gṛheṣu guṇitā goṣṭhīṣu vidyāvatāṃbhaktiḥ śrīpatipādaopallavanakhajyotsnāsu viśrāmyati ||3||pratyekaṃ viṣayeṣu pañcakamitaiḥ ślokaiḥ kavīnāmidaṃtenākāraṇabāndhavena vidadhe śrīsūktikarṇāmṛtam |prītiṃ pallavayantu karṇakalasīmāpūrayantaściraṃmajjantaḥ pariśīlayantu rasikāḥ pañca pravāhāniha ||4||amarāḥ śṛṅgāracaṭū apadeśoccāvace kramaśaḥ |iti pañcabhiḥ pravāhaiḥ saduktikarṇāmṛtaṃ kriyate ||5||---amarapravāhavīcayaḥatha dhātā ravirīśapraṇatimahādevaśivaharakrīḍāḥ |praśnottarāṭṭahāsāvamuṣya mūrdhīttamāṅgagaṅgā ca ||1||mauliśaśī koṭīro muṇḍāvalirakṣi purabhidārambhaḥ |bāṇānaloṣṭamūrtirbhairavaharatāṇḍavārambhau ||2||nṛtyaṃ haraprasādanamatha gaurī pariṇayasthagaurī ca |śṛṅgāro giriduhiturdurgā kālī tathārdhanārīśaḥ ||3||śṛṅgārī ca gajānanaśarasambhavabhṛṅgiṇaḥ pramathāḥ |atha hariharau sakāntau surasindhurjahnkanyakāśaṃsā ||4||matsyakamaṭhasūkarakeśarinṛsiṃhapāṇijanmānaḥ |śṛṅgārī ca nṛsiṃho vāmanamūrtistrivikramo bhṛgujaḥ ||5||dāśarathireṣa virahī haladharajinakalkino'tha kṛṣṇasya |śiśutākumārabhāvau svapnāyitayauvanakrīḍāḥ ||6||praśnottaraṃ ca veṇudhvananaṃ gītaṃ bhujaśca giridharaṇam |utkaṇṭhā gopavadhūsandeśo hariramuṣya bhaktiśca ||7||udadhimathanaharirambudhimathanotthaśrīḥ svayaṃvaro lakṣmyāḥ |śrī śṛṅgāraḥ kamalākamalopālabhavākpraśastenduḥ ||8||candrakalā śaśibimbaṃ prauḍhavidhuḥ sarucicandramā raśmiḥ |jyotsnā kalaṅkatamauḍukairavasahitendubhāvaśca ||9||miśrabahurūpakāstaṅgatabahuviṣayendavo'tha gandhavahaḥ |dakṣiṇanadīsamudraprabhātabhinnaśca puṣpadhanvā ca ||10||smaraśauryamathoccāvacamiti pañcopetanavativīcibhiḥ |śrīdharadāsena kṛtaḥ kṛtinā devapravāho'yam ||11||devapravāhaḥ1. atha brahmavīciḥśambhoḥ sākṣātsakhaikaḥ surapatiparo dharmarājastathānyaḥprāṇā viśvasya kasya prathamataramataḥ ko'nu sambhāṣaṇīyaḥ |kāryāyātānviditvā muhuriti caturo lokapālāṃścaturbhirvaktrairābhāṣamāṇaḥ samamuditaravaḥ pātu padmodbhavo vaḥ ||1||pālitasya |āgaskāriṇi kālanemidalane tattāḍanārthaṃ ruṣānābhīpaṅkajamastratāṃ gamayituṃ jāne prayatne śriyaḥ |āvāsonmathanopapāditabhayabhrāntātmanaḥ sambhramādabrahmaṇyaparāḥ purātanamunervācaḥ prasīdantu vaḥ ||2||bhaṭṭaśrīnivāsasya | (sū.mu. 2.108)pāyādvo madhukaiṭabhāsuravadhe viṣṇuprabodhoddhurodhātā vaktracatuṣṭayaṃ tu yugapadyasyābhavatsārthakam |ekaṃ stauti mukhaṃ śivāmitaradapyārtaṃ varānyācatedaityau pratyaparaṃ vitarjati haratyanyacchriyaḥ sambhramam ||3||vasantadevasya |yanna kṣuṇṇaṃ kadācittuhinakaṇacayasyandibhiścandrapādairnāpi vyālīnamusrairnavanalinasarobandhubhirbhānavīyaiḥ |tatkalpāntānuṣaṅgi drutamatanutamaḥ pāṭayantyaḥ samantādādyādhītau vidhāturmukhaśaśivisṛtāḥ pāntu vo dantabhāsaḥ ||4||bījakasya |jātaste'dharakhaṇḍanātparibhavaḥ kāpālikādyo'bhavatsa brahmādiṣu kathyatāmiti muhurbālyādguhe jalpati |gaurīṃ hastayugena ṣaṇmukhavaco roddhuṃ nirīkṣyākṣamāṃvailakṣyāccaturāsyaniṣphalaparāvṛttiściraṃ pātu vaḥ ||5||(su.ra. 101, sū.mu. 2.105)2. sūryaḥtuṅgodayādribhujagendraphaṇopalāyavyomendranīlatarukāñcanapallavāya |saṃsārasāgarasamutkramiyogisārthaprasthānapūrṇakalasāya namaḥ savitre ||6||varāhamihirasya | (su.ra. 150)viṣvagvisāritimiraprakarāvaruddhatrailokyanetrapuṭasiddharasāyanāya |tubhyaṃ namaḥ kamalaṣaṇḍaviṣādanidrāvidrāvaṇodyatakarāya divākarāya ||7||śrīkaṇṭhasya |śukatuṇḍacchavi savituścaṇḍarucaḥ puṇḍarīkavanabandhoḥ |maṇḍalamuditaṃ vande kuṇḍalamākhaṇḍalāśāyāḥ ||8||vidyāyāḥ | (su.ra. 149, śā.pa. 86)jīyādekaphalaṃ nabhastalatarorabhraṃśi sindūriṇīmudrā kairavakānanasya timirasteyāya sandhirdivaḥ |mandārastavakontarīkṣakavarībhārasya gaurīpateḥkampillacchadapāṭalacchavi kulacchatraṃ raghūṇāṃ raviḥ ||9||hareḥ |ādyūnastamasāṃ cakoraramaṇīrāgābdhimanthācalojīvāturjalajasya vāsavadiśāśailendracūḍāmaṇiḥ |ādeṣṭā śrutikarmaṇāṃ kumudinīśokāgnipūrṇāhutirdevaḥ somarasāyanaṃ vijayate viśvasya bījaṃ raviḥ ||10||vibhākarasya |3. īśapraṇatiḥmaulau vegādudañcatyapi caraṇabharanyañcadurvītalatvādakṣuṇṇasvargalokasthitimuditasuraśreṣṭhagoṣṭhīstutāya |saṃtrāsānniḥsaranatyavirataviṣajaddakṣiṇārdhāṅgabandhādatyaktāyādriputryā tirpuraharajagatkleśahantre namaste ||11||bāṇasya | (su.ra. 56)namastuṅgaśiraścumbicandracāmaracārave |trailokyanagarārambhamūlastambhāya śambhave ||12||(su.ra. 48)tādṛksaptasamudramudritamahībhūbhṛdbhirabhraṃkaṣaistāvadbhiḥ parivāritā pṛthudvīpaiḥ samantādiyam |yasya sphāraphaṇāmaṇau nilayanāttiryakkalaṅkākṛtiḥśeṣaḥ so'pyagamadyadaṅgadapadaṃ tasmai namaḥ śambhave ||13||ballaṇasya | (su.ra. 38)namastasmai kasmaicana vacanavittendriyayamīyamīśānaṃ jyotirmayamayamupāste munijanaḥ |gurūpajñaprajñāmukuranikurambapratiphalannijānandajyotsnābhyudayabhidurājñānatimiraḥ ||14||hareḥ |vṛṣadhana dhanadapriya priyārdhagrathanavidagdha vidagdhacittayone |purahara hariṇāṅkacūḍa cūḍābhujagabhayaṅkara dhūrjaṭe namaste ||15||bhojadevasya |4. mahādevaḥśilpaṃ trīṇi jaganti yasya kavitā yasya trivedī guroryaścakre tripuravyayaṃ tripathagā yanmūrdhni mālyāyate |trīnkālāniva vīkṣituṃ vahati yo visphūrjadakṣṇāṃ trayaṃsa traiguṇyaparicchedo vijayate devastriśūlāyudhaḥ ||16||vasukalpadattasya | (su.ra. 30)arvāñcatpañcaśākhaḥ sphuraduparijaṭāmaṇḍalaḥ saṃśritānāṃnityāparṇo'pi tāpatritayamapanayansthāṇuravyādapūrvaḥ |yaḥ pronmīlatkapardaiḥ śirasi viracitābālabandhe dyusindhoḥpāthobhirlabdhasekaḥ phalati phalaśataṃ vāñchitaṃ bhaktibhājām ||17||jahnoḥ |kāmaṃ mā kāmayadhvaṃ vṛṣamapi ca bhṛśaṃ mādriyadhvaṃ na vittecittaṃ datta śrayadhvaṃ paramamṛtaphalā yā kalā tāmihaikām |itthaṃ devaḥ smarārirvṛṣamadharacarīkṛtya mūrtyaiva ditsanniḥsvo viśvopadeśānamṛtakarakalāśekharastrāyatāṃ vaḥ ||18||kavipaṇḍitaśrīharṣasya |bhūtivyājena bhūmīmamarapurasaritkaitavādambu bibhrallālāṭākṣicchalena jvalanamahipatiśvāsalakṣyaṃ samīram |vistīrṇāghoravaktrodarakuharanibhenāmbaraṃ pañcabhūtairviśvaṃ śaśvadvitanvanvitaratu bhavataḥ sampadaṃ candramauliḥ ||19||jayadevasya |pīyūṣeṇa viṣeṇa tulyamaśanaṃ svarge śmaśāne sthitirnirbhedāḥ payaso'nalasya vahane yasyāviśeṣagrahaḥ |aiśvaryeṇa ca bhikṣayā ca gamayankālaṃ samaḥ sarvatodevaḥ svātmani kautukī haratu vaḥ saṃsārapāśaṃ haraḥ ||20||vaidyagadādharasya |5. śivaḥvedānteṣu yamāhurekapuruṣaṃ vyāpya sthitaṃ rodasīyasminnīśvara ityananyaviṣayaḥ śabdo yathārthākṣaraḥ |antaryaśca mumukṣubhirniyamitaprāṇādibhirmṛgyatesa sthāṇuḥ sthirabhaktiyogasulabho niḥśreyasāyāstu vaḥ ||21||kālidāsasya | (Vik. 1.1)kaṇṭhacchāyamiṣeṇa kalparajanīmuttaṃsamandākinīrūpeṇa pralayābdhimūrdhvanayanavyājena kalpājalam |bhūṣāpannagakelipānakapaṭādekonapañcāśataṃvātānapyupasaṃharannavatu vaḥ kalpāntaśāntau śivaḥ ||22||cittapasya |kvāpyagniḥ kvacidadribhūrnaraśiraḥkīrṇā kvacinnimnagārūkṣā kvāpi jaṭā kvacidviṣadharā raudraṃ viṣaṃ kutracita|tādṛgbhūtagaṇairvṛto mama citābhasmormikirmīritaḥsaṃsāraṃ pratimucya yāturapunaryogāya panthāḥ śivaḥ ||23||bilhaṇasya |nirmātā jagadarthameva vacasāṃ vācaṃ yamo yaḥ svayaṃbhogānviśvakṛte tanoti viṣayavyāvartitātmendriyaḥ |dhatte'strāṇi jaganti rakṣitumudāsīnaḥ svadehagraheyogīndro'stu sadāśivaḥ sa bhavatāṃ bhūtyai parārthavratī ||24||vaidyagadādharasya |dūronmuktakhageśvare murabhidi vyākṣiptabāhau grahavyūhe vāritamātariśvani namatyāśāpatīnāṃ gaṇe |niṣkamporagahāravalliracalaccūḍenduravyākulasvaḥsindhuḥ sthirayoganirvṛtamanāḥ pāyāttrilokīṃ śivaḥ ||25||tasyaiva |6. haraśṛṅgāraḥevaṃ sthāpaya subhru bāhulatikāmevaṃ kuru sthānakaṃnātyuccairnama kuñcitāgracaraṇaṃ māṃ paśya tāvatkṣaṇam |gaurīṃ nartayataḥ svavaktramurajenāmbhodharadhvānināśambhorvaḥ sukhayantu lambhitalayacchedāhatāstālikāḥ ||26||yogeśvarasya | (su.ra. 60)tasyā nāma mayā kathaṃ kathamapi bhrāntyā samuccāritaṃjānāsyeva mamāśayaṃ tava kṛte gauri prasannā bhava |kṣāntiḥ svīkriyatāṃ dayāvati mayi krodhaḥ parityajyatāmityevaṃ bahu jalpataḥ smararipoḥ premāñjaliḥ pātu vaḥ ||27||cakrapāṇeḥ |bālaḥ sundari candramāḥ srutasudhādhārābhirāpyāyitonidrāmeti phaṇīśvaraḥ suradhunī ruddhā jaṭāvallibhiḥ |itthaṃ manmathakelikautukavidhau vrīḍāvatīṃ pārvatīṃpāyādvaḥ pratibodhayannavavadhūṃ candrārdhacūḍāmaṇiḥ ||28||kakkolasya |śrutiḥ saktā mugdhe vacasi vadanendau nipatitādṛśaḥ svādau bimbādharamadhuni magnaiva rasanā |niṣaṇṇābhūnnāsā nijaparimale śailaduhiturghanāśleṣānande vapurapi vilīnaṃ purabhidaḥ ||29||umāpatidharasya |dūre dāruvanābhisāraka mṛṣā cāṭūni muñcādhunābhūyastvaṃ punarapyahaṃ yadi tadā candraḥ kṣitiṃ yāsyati |ityuktaḥ śaśimauliradrisutayā cūḍendubhūlambhanavyājavyañjitapādapadmapatanaprītapriyaḥ pātu vaḥ ||30||kavipaṇḍitaśrīharṣasya | (sū.mu. 2.8)7. śivayoḥ praśnottaramkasmātpārvati niṣṭhurāsi sahaja śailīdbhavānāmidaṃniḥsnehāsi kuto na bhasmaparuṣaḥ snehaṃ kvacinnindati |kopaste mayi niṣphalaḥ priyatame sthāṇau phalaṃ kiṃ bhaveditthaṃ nirvacanīkṛto dayitayā śambhuḥ śivāyāstu vaḥ ||31||bhojadevasya | (su.ra. 35)kiṃ gauri māṃ prati ruṣā nanu gauḥ kimasmikupyāmi kaṃ prati mayītyanumānato'ham |jānāmi satyamaunāmanata eva sa tvamitthaṃ giro giribhuvaḥ kuṭilā jayanti ||32||rudraṭasya | (Kāvyālaṅkāra 2.15, sū.mu. 99.6)keyaṃ mūrdhnyandhakāre timiramiha kutaḥ subhru kāntenduyuktekāntāpyatraiva kāminnanu jalamumayā pṛṣṭametāvadeva |nāhaṃ dvandvaṃ karomi vyapanaya śirasastūrṇamenāmidānīmevaṃ proktaṃ bhavānyā prativacanajaḍaḥ pātu vo manmathāriḥ ||33||kasyacita||eṣā te hara kā sugātri katamā mūrdhni sthitā kiṃ jaṭāhaṃsaḥ kiṃ bhajate jaṭāṃ na hi śaśī candro jalaṃ sevate |mugdhe bhūtiriyaṃ kuto'tra salilaṃ bhūtistaraṅgāyateitthaṃ yo vinigūhate tripathagāṃ pāyānsa vaḥ śṛṅgāraḥ ||34||kasyacita| (Sv67)dhanyā keyaṃ sthitā te śirasi śaśikalā kiṃ nu nāmaitadasyānāmaivāsyāstadetatparicitamapi te vismṛtaṃ kasya hetoḥ |nārīṃ pṛcchāmi nenduṃ kathayatu vijayā na pramāṇaṃ yadīndurdevyā nihnotumicchoriti surasaritaṃ śāṭhyamavyādvibhorvaḥ ||35||viśākhadattasya | (ṃudrārākṣas1.1, sū.mu. 99.1)8. harahāsyampāṇau kaṅkaṇamutphaṇaḥ phaṇipatirnetraṃ jvalatpāvakaṃkaṇṭhaḥ kuṇṭhitakālakūṭakuṭilo vastraṃ gajendrājinam |gaurīlocanalobhanāya subhago veṣo varasyeti megaṇḍollāsavibhāvitaḥ paśupaterhāsodgamaḥ pātu vaḥ ||36||rudraṭasya | (śṛ.ti. 3.2a)uddāmadantarucipallavitārdhacandrajyotsnānipītatimiraprakarāvarodhaḥ |śreyāṃsi vo diśatu tāṇḍavitasya śambhorambhodharāvalighanadhvaniraṭṭahāsaḥ ||37||saṅghamitrasya | (su.ra. 41)mātarbrūhi kimetadañjalipuṭe tātena gopāyitaṃvatsa svāduphalaṃ prayacchati na me gatvā gṛhāṇa svayam |mātraivaṃ prahite guhe vighaṭayatyākṛṣya sandhyāñjaliṃśambhorbhagnasamādhiruddhamanaso hāsyodgamaḥ pātu vaḥ ||38||yogeśvarasya | (su.ra. 59)nirvighnaṃ ghanasārasāraviśadasvarlokakallolinīkallolapratimallabāhucalanairvyāptāntarālaśriyaḥ |śambhoḥ sambhavadaṅgahārataralottaṃsāmṛtāṃśudravaprāṇātprāṇikapālacāpaladṛśo hāsormayaḥ pāntu vaḥ ||39||vācaspateḥ ||bhṛṅgī kastava carcike guha na ko'pyākāra ekastu nausatyaṃ bhṛṅgariṭe susatyamanṛtaṃ lokaṃ tu moṭirvadeta|nagnaṃ pṛcchatamastu vāṃ pariṇayaikātmatvamityudbhaṭastāvutsṛjya saparṣadaḥ paśupaterhāsyodgamaḥ pātu vaḥ ||40||9. haraśiraḥtvaṅgadgaṅgamudañcadinduśakalaṃ bhraśyatkapālāvalikroḍabhrāmyadamandamārutacayasphārībhavadbhāṅkṛti |pāyādvo ghanatāṇḍavavyatikaraprāgbhārakhedaskhaladbhogīndraślathapiṅgalotkaṭajaṭājūṭaṃ śiro dhūrjaṭeḥ ||41||vīryamitrasya | (su.ra. 42)sandhyātāṇḍavitasya khaṇḍaparaśoravyājjaganti jvalallālāṭākṣipuṭodbhavānalaśikhālīḍhendulekhaṃ śiraḥ |bhraśyatkṛtti calanmahāhivigaladvyomāpagāmbuskhalatkhaṇḍendūcchalabhūticaṭulabhrāmyajjaṭāsantati ||42||yogeśvarasya |tasyārdhaṃ kupitā haṭhādyadi harenmūrdhni sthitā jāhnavīhā nātha kva tadeti duḥsthahṛdayo bhṛṅgī bhṛśaṃ śuṣyati ||154||bhavānandasya |sevāṃ no kurute karoti na kṛṣiṃ vāṇijyamasyāsti nopaitryaṃ nāsti dhanaṃ na bāndhavabalaṃ naivāsti kaścidgaṇaḥ |dyūtastrīvyasanaṃ na muñcati tathāpīśastadasmātphalaṃkiṃ me syāditi cintayanniva kṛśo bhṅgī ciraṃ pātu vaḥ ||155||kasyacita|32. gaṇoccāvacamsthūlo dūramayaṃ na yāsyati kṛśo naiṣa prayāṇakṣamastenaikasya mamaiva tatra kaśipuprāptiḥ paraṃ dṛśyate |ityādau paricintitaṃ pratimuhustadbhṛṅgikūṣmāṇḍayoranyonyapratikūlamīśaśivayoḥ pāṇigrahe pātu vaḥ ||156||kasyacita| (su.ra. 99)carcāyāḥ kathameva rakṣati sadā sadyo nṛmuṇḍasrajaṃcaṇḍīkeśariṇo vṛṣaṃ ca bhujagānsūnormayūrādapi |ityantaḥparibhāvayanbhagavato dīrghaṃ dhiyaḥ kauśalaṃkūṣmāṇḍo dhṛtisambhṛtāmanudinaṃ puṣṇāti tundaśriyam ||157||kasyacita| (su.ra. 97)devī sūnumasūta nṛtyata gaṇāḥ kiṃ tiṣṭhatetyudbhujeharṣādbhṛṅgariṭāvayācitagirā cāmuṇḍayāliṅgite |avyādvo hatadundubhisvanaghanadhvānātiriktastayoranyonyapracalāsthitpañjararaṇatkaṅkālajanmā ravaḥ ||158||yogeśvarasya | (su.ra. 71, sū.mu. 2.55)śṛṅgaṃ bhṛṅginvimuñca tyaja gajavadana tvaṃ ca lāṅgūlamūlaṃmandānando'si nandinnalamabala mahākāla kaṇṭhagraheṇa |ityuktvā nīyamānaḥ sukhayatu vṛṣabhaḥ pārvatīpādamūlepaśyannakṣairvilakṣaṃ valitagalacalatkambalaṃ tryambakaṃ vaḥ ||159||abhinandasya | (su.ra. 77)digvāsā vṛṣavāhano naraśirodhārī dadhāno'jinaṃbhikṣurbhasmabhujaṅgabhūṣitatanurbhūtairbhramankānanam |smartèṇāṃ śivakṛttathāpi jagati jyeṣṭho'smadīyaḥ prabhurdhanyo'smītyatitoṣapuṣṭajaṭharaḥ kūṣmāṇḍako'vyājjagata||160||mahānidheḥ |33. hariharauyadbaddhārdhajaṭaṃ yadardhamukuṭaṃ yaccandramandārayordhatte dhāma ca dāma ca smitalasatkundendranīlaśriyoḥ |tatkhaṭvāṅgarathāṅgasaṅgavikaṭaṃ śrīkaṇṭhavaikuṇṭhayorvande nandimahokṣatārkṣyapariṣannāmāṅkamekaṃ vapuḥ ||161||rājaśekharasya | (su.ra. 1639)niyamitajaṭāvallīlīlāprasuptamahoragaṃcaraṇakamalaprānte muktasvavikramagovṛṣam |vitataphaṇibhukpatracchatraṃ gadālaguḍaśriyaṃhariharavapurbrahmopāsyaṃ punātu jagattrayam ||162||bhavānandasya |yena dhvastamanobhavena balijitkāyaḥ purāstrīkṛtoyo gaṅgāṃ ca dadhe'ndhakakṣayakaro yo barhipatrapriyaḥ |yasyāhuḥ śaśimacchiro hara iti stutyaṃ ca nāmāmarāḥso'vyādiṣṭabhujaṅgahāravalayastāṃ sarvado mādhavaḥ ||163||bhāraveḥ | (Sv44, sū.mu. 2.104, Sāh.d. 10.12)ekāvasthitirastu vaḥ puramurapradveṣiṇordevayoḥprāleyāñjanaśailaśṛṅgasubhagacchāyāṅgayoḥ śreyase |tārkṣyatrāsavihastapannagaphaṭā yasyāṃ jaṭāpālayobālendudyutikośasuptajalajo yasyāṃ ca nābhīhradaḥ ||164||tuṅgokasya |yajjambūkamburociḥ phaṇadharapariṣadbhojibhogīndrakāntaṃnandaccandrāravindadyuticaraṇaśiraḥsyandimandākinīkaṃ |rakṣāsaṃhāradakṣaṃ madanasamudayoddīpanaṃ śaśvadavyādavyāghātaṃ vibodhe'pyudadhigirisutākāntayordehamekam ||165||jalacandrasya |34. kāntāsahitahariharausambhogaspṛhayālumanmathapunarjanmāspadaṃ bhūrbhuvaḥsvaḥ pāyātpuruṣottamakratubhidorardhārdhapūrṇaṃ vapuḥ |yallakṣmīgirijākaṭākṣakuṭilakrīḍāhaṭhākṛṣṭibhiḥsyādeva truṭitaṃ parasparaguṇasyūtaṃ na cedantarā ||166||tripurāripālasya |vapuravatu jaṭākirīṭamiśraṃpuramurasūdanayorvimiśritaṃ vaḥ |girijalaghisutāsvabhartṛkaṇṭhagrahacalitāhṛtabāhuvallarīkam ||167||tasyaiva |sphaṭikamarakataśrīhāriṇoḥ prītiyogāttadavatu vapurekaṃ kāmakaṃsadviṣorvaḥ |na viramati bhavānyāḥ śvaḥśreyasāyāstu vaḥ |yasminbhūdharakanyakābdhisutayoraprāptasambhogayoranyonyapratikarmanarmabhiduro bhūyānanaṅgajvaraḥ ||169||hareḥ |dhātrā sauhṛdasīmavismitamukhaṃ bhedabhramāpāsanātsānandaṃ prakriyā kīdṛśīyam ||171||kolāhalasya |durvāradoṣatimirāgamavāsaraśrīḥkaivalyakairavavikāsasitāṃśulekhā |jīyāttriviṣṭapadhunī kalikālabhagnagīrvāṇarājanagarākaravaijayantī ||172||graheśvarasya |tīrthāṭanaiḥ kimadhikaṃ kṣaṇamīkṣitā cetpītaṃ tvadambu yadi devi mudhā sudhāpi |snātaṃ yadi tvayi viriñcipadaṃ na dūremuktiḥ kare yadi ca sā samupāsitāsi ||173||viriñceḥ |tīraṃ tavāvataratīha yathā yathaivadehena devi jaratā munajo mumūrṣuḥ |amba svayaṃvaravaśaṃvadanākanārīdorvallipallavi nabho'pi tathā tathaiva ||174||tasyaiva |taptaṃ yanna tapo hutaṃ ca na ||175||sentutasya |36. gaṅgāpraśaṃsādharmasyotsavavaijayantimukuṭasragveṇigaurīpatestvāṃ ratnākarapatni jahnutanaye bhāgīrathi prārthaye |tvattoyāntaśilāniṣaṇṇavapuṣastvadvīcibhiḥ karuṇā hīnā na dīnātmasu |prakṣīṇā kalikalmaṣakṣayakarī tṛṣṇā na kṛṣṇārcanedevi śraddadhatāṃ gatistvayi mudā mandā na mandākini ||177||tasyaiva |prasīda śrīgaṅge |baddhāñjalirnaumi kuru prasādamapūrvamātā bhava devi gaṅge |ante vayasyaṅgagatāya mahyamadehabandhāya payaḥ prayaccha ||180||kevaṭṭapapīpasya |37. harermatsyāvatāraḥmatsyaḥ punātu ||183||vasantadevasya |pātu trīṇi jaganti pārśvakaṣaṇaprakṣuṇṇadiṅmaṇḍalonaikābdhistimitodaraḥ sa bhagavānkrīḍājhaṣaḥ keśavaḥ |aparyāptajalakrīḍāraso diśatu vaḥ śivam ||185||kasyacita|38. kūrmaḥpṛṣṭhabhrāmyadamandamandaragirigrāvāgrakaṇḍūyanānnidrāloḥ kamaṭhākṛterbhagavataḥ śvāsānilāḥ pāntu vaḥ |cāpaṃ cāpaṃ na khaḍgaṃ jhaṭiti hahahahā karkaśatvaṃ nakhānāmityevaṃ daityarājaṃ nijanakhakuliśairjaghnivānso'vatādvaḥ ||200||śrīvyāsapādānām | (su.ra. 128, sū.mu. 2.76)41. |vyāvalgadbalavaddhiraṇyakaśipukroḍasthalīpāṭanaspaṣṭaprasphuṭadasthipañjararavakrūrā nakhāḥ pāntu vaḥ ||201||dakṣasya | (su.ra. 141)ye bālendukalārdhavibhramabhṛto māyānṛsiṃhākṛterniryātā iva 130)42. śṛṅgārinarasiṃhaḥlakṣmīmuraḥparisare vahataḥ salīlaṃyogāsanaṃ ca carato nṛharerjayanti |ekakṣaṇopanatamānmathabhāvamugdhasvātmāvabodhamasṛṇāni vilokitāni baliprārthanakṛtetrapālīnairaṅgairyadayamabhavadvāmanatanuḥ ||211||vaṅkasya |apasara pṛthivi samudrāḥ saṃvṛṇutāmbūni bhūbhṛto namata |vāmanaharilaghutunde jagatīkalahaḥ sa vaḥ pātu ||212||bhavānandasya |kutastvamaṇukaḥ svataḥ svamiti kiṃ na yatkasyacitkimicchasi padatrayaṃ nanu bhuvā kimityalpayā |dvijasya śamino mama tribhuvanaṃ tadityāśayoharerjayati nihnutaḥ prakaṭitaśca vakroktibhiḥ ||213||vākpateḥ | (su.ra. 114)pūjyo brahmavidāṃ tvameva vimalajñānaikapātraṃ bhavānmadbhāgyena gato'tithitvamadhunā kiṃ te tribhirbhūpadaiḥ |trailokyaṃ bhavataṃ ||215||gaṇādhyakṣasya | (śā.pa. 278)44. trivikramaḥkiṃ chatraṃ kiṃ nu ratnaṃ tilakamatha tathā kuṇḍalaṃ kaustubho vācakraṃ vā vārijaṃ vetyamarayuvatibhiryadbalidhvaṃsi dehe |ūrdhvaṃ maulau |cañcatpādanakhāgramaṇḍalaruciprasyanigaṅgājalovisphūrjadbalirājyanāśapiśunotpātāmbuvāhadyutiḥ |pātu tvāṃ caraṇo hareḥ kramavidhau yasyādhikaṃ dyotatedūrādaṅgulimudrikāmaṇiriva sphārāṅkuśajālo raviḥ ||218||vikramādityasya |yatkāṇḍaṃ gaganadrumasya yadapi kṣoṇītaḍāgodaredevasyaiva yaśo'mbuśobhini mahāyaṣṭiḥ pratiṣṭhākarī |tadviṣṇoḥ padamantarālajaladherādhārato bhūtalātpāraṃ dyāmupagantumudyamavatāṃ setūbhavatpātu vaḥ ||219||cakrapāṇeḥ |kharvagranthivimuktasandhivikasadvakṣaḥsphuratkaustubhaṃniryannābhisarojakuḍmalakuṭīgambhīrasāmaedhvani |pātrāvāptisamutsukena |śauryaṃ śatrukulakṣayāvadhi yaśo brahmāṇḍakhaṇḍāvadhityāgaḥ saptasamudramudritamahīnirvājadānāvadhiḥ |vryaṃ yantu girāṃ na tatpathi nanu vyaktaṃ hi tatkarmabhiḥsatyaṃ brahmataponidherbhagavataḥ under4.60, padyā. 372)54. kṛṣṇayauvanamsottāpaṃ jaratītbhiraphuṭarasaṃ bālābhirunmīlitaśvāsaṃ veśma suvāsinībhiradhikākṛtaṃ bhujiṣyājanaiḥ |pratyagraprakaṭīkṛtārti kulaṭāsārthena dṛṣṭaṃ |mandākṣaślathavallavānukaraṇakrīḍasya kaṃsadviṣolabdhaṃ yauvanamātrayā vijayate gambhīraśobhaṃ vapuḥ ||267||abhinandasya |vatsa tvaṃ navayauvano'si capalāḥ prāyeṇa gopastriyaḥkaṃso 1139)rajanikaramayūkhonnidranīlotpalālīparimalabahugandho badhurastatparāgaiḥ |kavalitaratikhedasvedabindurniśāntepulakayati tuṣārāsāravarṣī samīraḥ ||458||sarasiruhasya |rāmāṇāṃ śṛṅgārapravāhavīcayaḥvayasoḥ sandhirudañcadyuvabhāvā yuvatiraṅganāścaryam |mugdhā madhyā prauḍhā navapariṇītā ca saiva visrabdhā ||1||garbhavatī satyavatī svairiṇyupadeśaguptabandhakyau |vaidagdhyavatī kulaṭā lakṣitakulaṭā ca vāravanitā ca ||2||api dākṣiṇātyapāścātyaudīcyaprācyayuvatayo grāmyāḥ |strīmātraṃ khaṇḍitayā sahānyasaṃbhogacihnadūnā ca ||3||kalitavirahiṇī virahiṇyasyā ||7||tasyāḥ priyasaṃvādo'vasthākathanaṃ pratīkṣaṇaṃ patyuḥ |kākaḥ priyasaṃbhedo'pyathābhisārakriyārambhaḥ ||8||abhisārikā dinatamojyotsnādurdinagatā ca kulaṭānām |pralapitamabalārūpaṃ |yātrābhaṅgo viraho virahistrīsmaraṇamavalokaḥ ||11||citraṃ svapno yūnorabhilāṣastānavaṃ guṇākhyānam |udvegaḥ paridevanamidnusmarajalamucāmupālambhaḥ ||12||unmādaḥ smaralekhaḥ ||14||parirambhacumbanādharadaṃśanakhanyāsakaṇṭhakūjaśca |vastrākarṣanavoḍhāsaṃbhogau nidhuvanārambhaḥ ||15||surataṃ viparītarataṃ viparītaratānukathanasuratāntau |uṣasi priyāvalokanamatha |pāpasyāsya phalaṃ tadetadadhunā yaccandanendudyutiprāleyāmbusamīrapaṅkajavisairgātraṃ muhurdahyate ||674||rudraṭasya | (śṛ.ti. 1.77a, sū.mu. 56.1)dahati viraheṣvaṅgānīrṣyāṃ karoti kalahāntaritāvākyamsakhi sa subhago mandasneho mayīti na me vyathāvidhiviracitaṃ yasmātsarvo janaḥ sukhamaśnute |mama tu manasaḥ santāpo'yaṃ jane vimukho'pi yatkathamapi hatavrīḍaṃ ceto na yāti virāgitām ||676||amaroḥ | (Sv1118, su.ra. 694)niḥśvāsā vadanaṃ dahanti hṛdayaṃ nirmūlamunmathyatenidrā neti na dṛśyate priyamukhaṃ rātrindivaṃ rudyate |aṅgaṃ śoṣamupaiti pādapatitaḥ preyāṃstathopekṣitaḥsakhyaḥ kaṃ guṇamākalayya dayite mānaṃ vayaṃ kāritāḥ ||677||kasyacita| (amaru 98; padyā.. 237, da.rū. 2.26)jyotirbhyastadidaṃ tamaḥ samuditaṃ jāto'yamadbhyaḥ śikhīpīyūṣādidamutthitaṃ viṣamayaṃ chāyāptajanmātapaḥ |ko nāmāsya vidhiḥ praśāntiṣu bhavedbāḍhaṃ draḍhīyān ayaṃgranthiryatpriyato'pi vipriyamidaṃ sakhyaḥ kṛtaṃ sāntvanaiḥ ||678||kasyacita| (sa.ka.ā. 2.63)tallākṣālipilāñchitādapi mukhādinduḥ sa kiṃ duḥsahaḥsaṃtāpāya pikadhvaniḥ kimu mṛṣā vācāṃ prapañcādapi |kiṃ tasya praṇayāvadhīraṇaparādhīnādapi prekṣaṇādunmīlanti sakhi prasūnadhanuṣo marmacchidaḥ sāyakāḥ ||679||jalacandrasya |kathābhirdeśānāṃ kathamapi ca kālena bahunāsamāyāte kānte sakhi rajanirardhaṃ gatavatī |tato yāvallīlākalahakupitāsmi priyatamesapatnīva prācī digiyamabhavattāvadaruṇā ||680||kasyacita| (su.ra. 1642)42. kalahāntaritāsakhīvacanamanālocya premṇaḥ pariṇatimanādṛtya suhṛdastvayākāṇḍe mānaḥ kimiti sarale preyasi kṛtaḥ |samākṛṣṭā hyete virahadahanodbhāsuraśikhāḥsvahastenāñgārāstadalamadhunāraṇyaruditaiḥ ||681||amaroḥ (amaru 66; Sbhv1170; sū.mu. 56.9, su.ra. 659)mayā prāgevoktaṃ kalahavati mā tyājaya guṇaṃbhayestu preyāṃste svakaravaśagaṃ muñcasi mudhā |avāpto vailakṣyaṃ śara iva punarnaiti tadayaṃsvayaṃ gatvāneyaḥ priyasakhi karākarṣavidhinā ||682||ācāryagopīkasya |śravasi na kṛtāste tāvantaḥ sakhīvacanakramāścaraṇapatitoṅguṣṭhāgreṇāpyayaṃ na hato janaḥ |kaṭhinahṛdaye mithyāmaunavratavyasanādayaṃparijanaparityāgopāyo na mānaparigrahaḥ ||683||kasyacita| (su.ra. 687)jaghanamunnatamākulamekhalaṃmukhamapāṅgavisarpitatārakam |idamapāsya gato yadi nirghṛṇonanu vororu sa eva hi vañcitaḥ ||684||kasyacita| (Sv1168)sakhi na gaṇitā mānonmeṣātpriyapraṇayakṣatiḥparamiha sakhīvargasyedaṃ vaco na puraskṛtam |udayaśikharārūḍhe nāyaṃ kalānidhinā balātkimiti śithilo mānagranthiḥ karairna kariṣyate ||685||jalacandrasya |43. gotraskhalitampurastanvyā gotraskhalanacakito'haṃ natamukhaḥpravṛtto vailakṣyātkimapi likhituṃ daivahatakaḥ |sphuṭo rekhānyāsaḥ kathamapi sa tādṛkpariṇatogatā yena vyaktaṃ punaravayavaiḥ saiva taruṇī ||686||amaroḥ (amaru 46)kṛthā maivaṃ cetaḥ kathamapi manāgaskhaladitaḥpramādādvāṇīyaṃ kimiha karavāṇi praṇayini |vṛthaivāyaṃ granthirjhaṇajhaṇitamañjīraraṇitaṃtatastvatpādābjaṃ yadidamavataṃso bhavatu me ||687||narasiṃhasya |ardhokte bhayamāgato'si kimidaṃ kaṇṭhaśca kiṃ gadgadaścāṭorasya na ca kṣaṇo'yamanupakṣipteyamāstāṃ kathā |brūhi prastutamastu saṃprati mahatkarṇe sakhīnāṃ mukhaistṛptirnirbharamebhirakṣarapadaiḥ prāgeva me saṃbhṛtā ||688||abhinandasya | (sū.mu. 57.26)kathamapi kṛtapratyāpattau priye skhalitottarevirahakṛśayā kṛtvā vyājaṃ prakalpitamaśrutam |asahanasakhīśrotraprāptiṃ viśaṅkya sasaṃbhramaṃvivalitadṛśā śūnye gehe samucchvasitaṃ punaḥ ||689||kasyacita| (ās63)dūrādetya dṛśā nivārya ca sakhīrutkṣiptadoḥkaṅkaṇaśroṇiḥ sapraṇayā pidhāya nayanadvandvaṃ tavāvasthitā |jñātāsīti vipakṣanāma gadatā sambhāvitā sā tvayājīvatyeva yadi tvarāṃ tyaja nanu tvāmeva yāciṣyate ||690||ācāryagopīkasya |44. māninībāle nātha vimuñca mānini ruṣaṃ roṣānmayā kiṃ kṛtaṃkhedo'smāsu na me'parādhyati bhavānsarve'parādhā mayi |tatkiṃ rodiṣi gadgadena vacasā kasyāgrato rudyatenanvetanmama kā tavāsmi dayitā nāsmītyato rudyate ||691||amaroḥ (amaru 53; da.rū. 2.17; Sv1614, śā.pa. 3554, sū.mu. 57.1, su.ra. 653)ekatrāsanasaṃsthitiḥ parihatā pratudgamāddūratastāmbūlānayanacchalena rabhasāśelṣo'pi saṃvighnitaḥ |ālāpo'pi na miśritaḥ parijanaṃ vyāpārayantyāntikekāntaṃ pratyupacārataścaturayā kopaḥ kṛtārthīkṛtaḥ ||692||tasyaiva (amaru 17, su.ra. 639, Sv1583, śā.pa. 3534, sū.mu. 55.6, da.rū. 2.19, ṟask2.67g)āśaṅkya praṇatiṃ paṭāntapihitau pādau karotyādarātvyājenāgatamāvṛṇoti hasitaṃ na spaṣṭamudvīkṣate |mayyālāpavati pratīpavacanaṃ sakhyā sahābhāṣatetasyāstiṣṭhatu nirbharapraṇayitā māno'pi ramyodayaḥ ||693||tasyaiva (Sv. 1590, śā.pa. 3537, sū.mu. 55.11)dhūmāyate manasi mūrcchati ceṣṭiteṣusaṃdīpyate vapuṣi cetasi jājvalīti |vaktre parisphurati vāci vijṛmbhate'syāḥkāntāvamānajanito bahumānavahniḥ ||694||kasyacita|bāṣpāsāraḥ kathayati bhṛśaṃ gaṇḍayoḥ pāṇḍimānaṃśvāso bhūmnā stanakalasayoḥ pīnatāmātanoti |cittautsukyaṃ kimapi kurute kṣāmamaṅgaṃ tadasyāstāruṇyasya prasamadhikaṃ manyurāviṣkaroti ||695||kasyacita|45. udāttamāninīna mando vaktrenduḥ śrayati na lalāṭaṃ kuṭilatāṃna netrābjaṃ rajyatyanuṣajati na bhrūrapi bhidām |idaṃ tu preyasyāḥ prathayati ||699||kasyacita|yadyapi śriyamādhatte bhūṣaṇānādarastava |tathāpyantargataṃ manyumayaṃ kathayatīva me ||700||kasyacita|46. anuraktamāninīvalatu taralā dhṛṣṭā dṛṣṭiḥ khalā sakhi ||702||tasyaiva (amaru 24; su.ra. 695, Sbh1580; u.nī. 5.25)bhrūbhedo racitaḥ ciraṃ nayanayorabhyastamāmīlanaṃroddhuṃ śikṣitamādareṇa hasitaṃ maune'bhiyogaḥ kṛtaḥ |dhairyaṃ kartumapi (su.ra. 651)49. anunayaḥrambhoru kṣipa locanārdhamabhito bāṇānvṛthā manmathaḥsaṃdhattāṃ dhanurujjhatu kṣaṇamito bhrūvallimullāsaya |kiṃ cāntarnihitānurāgamadhurāmavyaktavarṇakramāṃmugdhe su.ra. 664, sa.ka.ā.v489, Sv1627)50. mānabhaṅgaḥdṛṣṭe locanavanmanāṅmukulitaṃ pārśvasthite vaktravannyagbhūtaṃ bahirāsitaṃ pulakavatsparśaṃ samātanvati |nīvībandhavadāgataṃ śithilatāṃ |māninyāścaraṇānativyatikare bāṣpāmbupūrṇekṣaṇaṃcakṣurjātamaho prapañcacaturaṃ jātāgasi preyasi ||724||tasyaiva | (amaru 44, sū.mu. 55.3, su.ra. 641)sutanu jahihi kopaṃ paśya pādānataṃ māṃna pravasadbhartṛkādṛṣṭaḥ kātaranetrayā cirtaraṃ baddhāñjaliṃ yācitpaścādaṃśukapallavena vidhṛto nirvyājamāliṅgitaḥ |ityākṣipya yadā samastamaghṛṇo gantuṃ pravṛttaḥ śaṭhaḥpūrvaṃ prāṇaparigraho kathyatāmudvignā kimakāṇḍa eva bhavatī tūṣṇīṃ kimevaṃ sthitā |pūrvoktyoparatāṃ priyeṇa dayitāmāśliṣya tattatkṛtaṃdatto yena samastapānthanivahaprāṇāntiko ḍiṇḍimaḥ ||728||kasyacita| (Sv1062)āpṛṣṭāsi vinirgato'dhvagajanastanvaṅgi gacchāmyahaṃsvalpaireva dinaiḥ samāgama iti jñātvā śucaṃ mā kṛthāḥ |ityākarṇya vacaḥ priyasya sahasā tanmugdhayā |ityākarṇya viyogamugdhamanasaḥ svapnopanītaṃ vacaḥsaṃjātā dayitasya yojanaśataṃ śayyopakaṇṭhasthalī ||730||jalacandrasya |52. yātrākṣepaḥkānte katyapi vāsarāṇi gamaya tvaṃ mīlayitvā ||789||ācāryagopīkasya |divase'pi dhūmamahiṣīvādyotsavadurdineṣu militāyāḥ |nākṛtapuṇyaḥ paśyasirahasi mudā vadanakramameṇākṣyāḥ ||790||umāpatidharasya |64. ||795||amaroḥ |65. jyotsnābhisārikāśaśadharakaraspardhāmugdhaṃ vidhāya vibhūṣaṇaṃkimiti valitagrīvaṃ mugdhe mudhaiva vilokyate |kṛtamapi kṛaṃ nedaṃ dūti pratīhi na māmiyaṃsahajamalinā svaḥsindhusaṃbandhinaḥprāleyācalabandhavastava guṇāḥ kairneha karṇārpitāḥ ||1388||hareḥ |devasya tripurārihāsamahasi prastūyamāne guṇeprītyā ca śrutikautukena ca balādākṛṣyamāṇaḥ svayam |ekaṃ saṃnatapakṣma pannagapatirdhatte sahasraṃ dṛśāmanyanmantharatārakāviluṭhanādatyantavisphāritama||1389||kasyāpi |merurdaṇḍo yadi ca paṭalaṃ medinīmaṇḍalaṃ syāccheṣaḥ sūtraṃ samadharaṇamapyeṣa vindhyo mahīdhraḥ |tanmātā ca tripuravijayī keśavo vā yadā syādunmīyeta kṣitipatanaya tvadguṇānāṃ samūhaḥ ||1390||pravarasenasya |5. dharmaḥbhrāntaṃ yena caturbhireva caraṇaiḥ satyābhidhāne yugetretāyāṃ tribhiraṅghribhiḥ kathamapi dvābhyāṃ tato dvāpare |na syāstvaṃ yadi deva paṅgulaguṅdaḥ kāle kalāvutkaleso'yaṃ paṅguravasthitaikacaraṇo dharmaḥ kathaṃ bhrāmyati ||1391||kasyacita| (su.ra. 1455, cittūkasya)ucchanneva kalau vṛṣasya caraṇaśreṇī navīnāṃ punastāṃ nirmāya kṛtastvayā punarapi nyastaḥ padasyandanaḥ |bhindānaistaraṇiṃ tvadastraniyatairetatkilodīritaṃśrutvānūrurasau vihāya mihiraṃ tvāṃ deva seviṣyate ||1392||ācāryagopīkasya |padaiścaturbhiḥ sukṛte sthirīkṛtekṛte'munā kena tapaḥ prapedire |bhuvaṃ yadekāṅghrikaniṣṭhayā spṛśandadhāvadharmo'pi kṛśastapasvitām ||1393||śrīharṣasya | (ṇc1.7)yūpairutkaṭakaṇṭakairiva makhaprodbhūtadhūmodgamairapyandhaṃkaraṇauṣadhairiva pade netre ca jātavyathaiḥ |yasmindharmapare praśāsati tapaḥsaṃbhedinīṃ medinīmāstāmākramituṃ vilokitumapi vyaktaṃ na śaktaḥ kaliḥ ||1394||jayadevasya |aśrāntaviśrāṇitayajñayūpastambhāvalīrdrāgavalambamānaḥ |yasya svabhāvādbhuvi saṃcacārakālakramādekapado'pi dharmaḥ ||1395||umāpatidharasya |6. rūpaṃśrīmadrūpaviṭaṅkadeva sakalakṣmāpālacuḍāmaṇeyuktaṃ saṃcaraṇaṃ yadatra bhavataścandreṇa rātrāvapi |mā bhūttvadvadanāvalokanavaśādvrīḍāvilakṣaḥ śaśīmā bhūcceyamarundhatī bhagavatī duḥśīlatābhājanam ||1396||tribhuvanasarasvatyāḥ |āvaktrendu tadaṅgameva sṛjataḥ sraṣṭuḥ samagrastviṣāṃkoṣaḥ śoṣamagādagādhajagatīśilpe'pi nālpāyitaḥ |niḥśeṣadyutimaṇḍalavyayavaśādīṣallabhaistattanūśeṣaḥ keśamayaḥ kimandhatamasastomairabhūnnirmitaḥ ||1397||śrīharṣasya |etatte mukhamakṣatendulaḍahacchāyaṃ |tairetatsamalaṅkṛtaṃ nijakulaṃ kiṃ vā bahu brūmaheye dṛṣṭāḥ parameśvareṇa bhavatā tuṣṭena ruṣṭena vā ||1404||jayādityasya | (su.ra. 1410, śā.pa. 1224)teṣāṃ dvāri dviradapatayastadvaśā ca madhyadeśamacirātkāñcyāṃ karaḥ pātitonitvaivaṃ vaśatāṃ priyeṇa bhavatābhīkena bhūrbhujyate ||1442||śabdārṇavasya |deva tvaṃ kila kuntalagraharuciḥ kāñcīmapāsārayankṣiptaḥ kṣiptakaragrahaḥ ||1444||śaraṇadevasya |tvaṃ colollolalīlāṃ kalayasi kuruṣe karṣaṇaṃ kuntalānāṃtvaṃ kāñcinyañcanāya prabhavati rabhasādaṅgasaṅgaṃ karoṣi |itthaṃ rājendra vandistutibhirupahitotkampamevādya dīrghaṃnārīṇāmapyarīṇāṃ hṛdayamudayate tvatpadārādhanāya ||1445||jayadevasya |16. dānaṃkatiṣu na kṛtā sevā ke vā na vāgvibhavaiḥ stutāstṛṇamapi guṇaprītaḥ prādānna ko'pi vipaścitām |ayamiha paraṃ duḥkhajvālākalāpamakhaṇḍayatkanakapayasāṃ dhārādaṇḍairakāṇḍaghanāghanaḥ ||1446||silhanasya |pūrṇo'gre kalaso vilāsavanitā smerānanā kanyakādānaklinnakapolapaddhatiribho ||1448||rājokasya |vāsaḥ svarṇagṛheṣu sakhyamamaraiḥ kalpadrumāṇāṃ vanekrīḍā svargavadhūgaṇaiḥ saha sudhākaṇṭhaṃ mudā pīyate |ruṣṭenedamakāri deva bhavatā hatvā raṇe vairiṇāṃtuṣṭaḥ preṣyajanāya vedmi na paraṃ gauḍendra kiṃ dāsyasi ||1449||dharmayogeśvarasya |tvannetre'pi tavānane'pi bhavataḥ pāṇāvapi tvatpade'pyasti smerasarojasauhṛdasamākṛṣṭaiva padmālayā |yannītā nijabhāvamarthibhirasau tvaddṛṣṭipātaistvadādeśāttvatkaravibhramairapi bhavatpādaprasādādapi ||1450||śaraṇasya |17. daridrabharaṇamyeṣāṃ veśamasu ||1451||bhāsokasya | (su.ra. 1394, kasyacit)karpāsāsthipracayanicitā nirdhanaśrotriyāṇāṃyeṣāṃ vātyāpravitatakuṭīprāṅgaṇāntā babhūvuḥ |tatsaudhānāṃ parisarabhuvi ||1467||laṅgadattasya |vāhū dvāvidamekameva bhuvanaṃ kastatra vīro rasaḥsāmrājyasya ca pūrvapūruṣabhujakṣuṇṇasya kiṃ na priyam |ityūrjasvalapauruṣasya puruṣaprāyaṃ jagatpaśyatoyasyātmāpi na yaśaḥ ||1609||rājaśekharasya | (su.ra. 1000)muktāśīkaranirjharāsu sadasi kṣuṇṇāsu kumbhasthalīṣvādantaḥ sphuṭakarṇacāmaradṛśāsvāvarjināṃ dantinām |kṣetrīkṛtya varūthinīṃ yudhi jayaśrīkarṣakeṇa dviṣāṃyenoptā iva muṣṭibhirnijayaśobījacchaṭā rejire ||1610||bhikṣoḥ |49. praśastayaśaḥākṣiptā cāmaraśrīḥ prasabhamapahṛtaḥ pauṇḍarīko vilāsaḥpracchanno vīrakambuḥ samajani vihitaḥ kaṇṭhabhārāya hāraḥ |lupto hāsaprakāśaḥ kamapi paribhavaṃ prāpitaḥ puṣparāśiścandrābhairyadyaśobhiḥ pratidharaṇibhujāṃ nihnutā kiṃ ca kīrtiḥ ||1611||śrīmatkeśavasenadevasya |ambhodhikṣiptamuktāruciharicaraṇodgīrṇagaṅgāmbutulyaṃkālindīphenakāntisphuritaphaṇadharonmuktanirmokarociḥ |karṇāṭīkuntalāntarvigalitasumanodāmaramyaṃ samantācchrīkhaṇḍālepalakṣmīmupanayati yaśo yasya khaḍgaprasūtam ||1612||jalacandrasya |bhūcakraṃ kiyadetadāvṛtamabhūdyadvāmanasyāṅghriṇānāgānāṃ kiyadāspadaṃ yadurasā laṅghanti gūḍhāṅghrayaḥ |ekāhādyadanūrurañcati kiyanmātraṃ tadapyambaraṃyasyetīva yaśo hriyā tribhuvanaṃ vyāpyāpi no tṛpyati ||1613||umāpatidharasya |gṛhādgṛhamupāgataṃ vrajati pattanaṃ pattanādvanāddhanamanudrutaṃ bhramati pādapaṃ pādapāta|girergirimadhiśritaṃ tarati vāridhiṃ vāridheryadīyamarisundarīnikarapṛṣṭhalagnaṃ yaśaḥ ||1614||tasyaiva |āste dāmodarīyāmiyamudaradarīṃ yāvalambya trilokīsaṃmātuṃ śaknuvanti prathimabharavaśādatra naitadyaśāṃsi |tāmetāṃ pūrayitvā niraguriva madhudhvaṃsinaḥ pāṇḍupadmacchadmāpannāni tāni dvipadaśanasanābhīni nābhīpathena ||1615||kavipaṇḍitaśrīharṣasya | (ṇc12.95, Sv2520, sū.mu. 97.23)50. kīrtiḥkā tvaṃ, kuntalamallakīrtir, ahaha kvāsi sthitā, na kvacitsakhyastāstava kutra kutra vada vāglakṣmīsrucaḥ samprati |vāgyātā caturānanasya vadanaṃ lakṣmīrmurāreruraḥkāntirmaṇḍalamaindavaṃ mama punarnādyāpi viśrāmabhūḥ ||1616||chittapasya | (su.ra. 1005)rāmaḥ sainyasamanvitaḥ kṛtaśilāseturyadambhonidheḥpāraṃ laṅghitavānpurā tadadhunā nāścaryamutpādayeta|ekākinyapi setubandharahitānsaptāpi vārāṃ nidhīnhelābhistava deva kīrtivanitā yasmātsamullaṅghati ||1617||tasyaiva | (su.ra. 1012)kiṃ vṛttāntaiḥ paragṛhagataiḥ kiṃtu nāhaṃ samarathastūṣṇīṃ sthātuṃ prakṛtimukharo dākṣiṇātyasvabhāvaḥ |deśe deśe vipaṇiṣu tathā catvare pānagoṣṭhyāmunmatteva bhramati bhavato vallabhā hanta kīrtiḥ ||1618||tutātitasya | (Sv2544, su.ra. 996, śā.pa. 1227)anantāsau kīrtiḥ kavikumudabandhoḥ kṣitipatestrilokīyaṃ kṣudrā tadiha kathamasyāḥ sthitiriti |mudheyaṃ vaḥ śaṅkā kalayata kiyaddarpaṇatalaṃviśālā kiṃ tatra sphurati na kavīndrapratikṛtiḥ ||1619||pañcākṣarasya |dhyāyantī nirapāyanāyakaguṇaṃ tvatkīrtirambhonidherbhrāmyanitvipināntareṣu virahavyagreva pāṇḍucchaviḥ |candraṃ nindati candanaṃ na sahate dveṣṭi śriyaṃ śāradīṃdūrādeva nirākaroti karakākarpūrahārasrajaḥ ||1620||śaraṇasya |51. savīryakīrtiḥvīrakṣīrasamudrasāndralaharīlāvaṇyalakṣmīmusastvatkīrtestulanāṃ kalaṅkamalino dhatte kathaṃ candramāḥ |syādevaṃ tvadarātisaudhaśikharaprodbhūtaśaṣpāṅkuragrāsavyagramanāḥ patedyadi punastasyāṅkaśāyī mṛgaḥ ||1621||śākyarakṣitasya | (sū.mu. 97.30)niḥsṛtyāhavasāgarādatha punaḥ saṃsṛtya pṛthvītalaṃkṛtvādho himaśailamīśvaraśiraḥśītāṃśulekhāmapi |gaṅgeva smṛtajanmabhūmiramaraiḥ sāścaryamālokitākīrtiste pratilomalaṅghitaviyadbrahmāṇḍamārohati ||1622||vākpateḥ | (sū.mu. 97.44)āsīduptaṃ yadetadraṇabhuvi bhavatā vairimātaṅgakumbhānmuktābījaṃ vimuktaṃ trijagati janayāmāsa kīrtidrumaṃ te |śeṣo mūlaṃ prakāṇḍaṃ himagirirudadhirdugdhapūrālavālaṃjyotsnā śākhāpratānaḥ kusumamuḍucayā yasya candraḥ phalaṃ ca ||1623||hareḥ | (su.ra. 1006)ekā gaṅgā prayāge malayaparisare candanaṃ mauktikālīkāntākaṇṭhe himāṃśurviyati sarasi śvetamabjaṃ tathāsyāḥ |kālindī kālasarpā marakatataralo lāñchanaṃ bhṛṅgamāletyevaṃ te yatra kīrtiḥ pariṇamati yutā yatra śatrorakīrtyā ||1624||rāmasya |sā candrādapi candanādapi daravyākoṣakundādapikṣīrābdherapi śeṣato'pi praśastakīrtiḥantaḥsantoṣabāṣpaiḥ sthagayati nayanaṃ na śrutibhraṃśabhīrurnāṅgenānastiromā racayati pulakaśreṇimānandakandām |na kṣoṇībhaṅgabhīruḥ kalayati ca śiraḥkampanaṃ tanna vidmaḥśṛṇvannetasya kīrtīḥ kathamuragapatiḥ prītimāviṣkaroti ||1626||kavipaṇḍitaśrīharṣasya | (ṇc12.39, sū.mu. 97.24)kṣīrodanvānalīkaḥ ||1627||vasukalpasya |kailāse nihnutaśrīḥ pariphitavapuḥ pārvaṇaḥ śvetabhānuḥśeṣaḥ pracchannaveśaḥ kalayati na ruciṃ jāhnavīvāriveṇiḥ |pītaḥ kṣīrāmburāśiḥ prasabhamapahṛtaḥ kuñjaro devabharturyatkīrtīnāṃ vivartairajani sa bhagavānekadanto'pyadantaḥ ||1628||śrīmatkeśavasenadevasya |yadvartmodyāti roddhuṃ tripuraharagirigrāmaṇīstanniyantuṃkauverīṃ kumbhajanmā vrajati yadi 1007)asya kṣoṇipateḥ parārdhaparayā lakṣīkṛtāḥ saṃkhyayāprajñācakṣuravekṣyamāṇatimiraprakhyāḥ kilākīrttayaḥ |gīyante svaramaṣṭamaṃ kalayatā jātena vandhyodarānmūkānāṃ prakareṇa kūrmaramaṇīdugdhodadheḥ rodhasi ||1635||kavipaṇḍitaśrīharṣasya | (Kuval, p. 146, ṇc12.106)54. uccāvacacāṭuḥabhyuddhṛtā vasumatī dalitaṃ ripūraḥkrīḍīkṛtā balavatā balirājalakṣmīḥ |ekatra janmani kṛtaṃ tadanena yūnājanmatraye yadakarotpuruṣaḥ purāṇaḥ ||1636||śrīhanūmataḥ | (sa.ka.ā. 1.98, V 471, sū.mu. 97.5)karṇaṃ cakṣurajīgaṇattava pitustātaḥ pitā te punaḥśaktyādhārakumāramapyajagaṇattaṃ kātaratvena saḥ |devo'gānmahiṣīti paśyati jagattvevaṃ vivektuṃ punaḥprāgalbhyaṃ prathayanti vastadapi ca prajñādhanāḥ sādhavaḥ ||1637||vidyāpateḥ |prabhurasi vayaṃ mālākāravratavyavasāyinovacanakusumaṃ tenāsmābhistavādaraḍhaukitam |yadi tadguṇaṃ kaṇṭhe mā dhāstathorasi mā kṛthānavamiti kiyatkarṇau dhehi kṣaṇaṃ phalatu śramaḥ ||1638||vīryamitrasya | (su.ra. 1418)vaktraṃ sākṣātsarasvatyadhivasati sadā śoṇa evādharastebāhuḥ kākutsthavīryasmṛtikaraṇapaṭurdakṣiṇaste samudraḥ |vāhinyaḥ pārśvametāḥ kṣaṇamapi bhavato naiva |cāṭupravāha īpsitaphalaprado bhavatu saṃtataṃ kṛtinām ||iti śrīmahāmāṇḍalikaśrīdharadāsakṛtau saduktikarṇāmṛte |cāṭupravāho nāma tṛtīyaḥ |( vīcayaḥ 54 | ślokāḥ 270 ||)-------------------------------------saduktikarṇāmṛtam**(4) **1. vāsudevaḥbhūtā eva timiṅgilaprabhṛtayo ye yādasāmagrimāste vaisāriṇaveśakeśavaśiśorjātā na rātrau punaḥ |pṛṣṭhaproñchitatoyatucchajaladherāpūrya yenāntaraṃtāḥ kallolaparamparā iva paraṃ dehatvaco darśitāḥ ||1641||kṣiyākasya |bhramati girirāṭpṛṣṭhe garjatyupaśruti sāgarodahati vitatajvālājālo jaganti viṣānalaḥ |sa tu vinihitagrīvākāṇḍaḥ kaṭāhapuṭāntaresvapiti bhagavānkūrmo nidrābharālasalocanaḥ ||1642||cirantanaśaraṇasya | (su.ra. 118, sū.mu. 108.2)jāyante bahavo'tra kacchapakule kiṃ tu kvacitkacchapīnaikāpyekamasūta sūnumaparaṃ sūtena vā soṣyate |ākalpaṃ dharaṇīdharodvahanataḥ santāpakhinnātmanoyaḥ kūrmasya dināni nāma katicidviśrāmadānakṣamaḥ ||1643||śatānandasya | (su.ra. 1105)niṣkandāmaravindinīṃ sthapuṭitoddeśāṃ sthalīṃ palvalejambālāvilamambu kartumaparā sūte varāhī sutāna|daṃṣṭrāyāṃ caturarṇavormitpaṭalairāplāvitāyāmiyaṃyasyā eva śiśoḥ sthitā vipadi bhūḥ sā putriṇī potriṇī ||1644||abhinandasya | (sa.ka.ā. 4.94, śā.pa. 1214, sū.mu. 36.6)apatyāni prāyo daśa daśa varāhī janayatikṣamābhāre dhuryaḥ sa punariha nāsīnna bhavitā |padaṃ kṛtvā yaḥ svaṃ phaṇipatiphaṇācakravalayenimajjantīmantarjaladhi vasudhāmudvalayati ||1645||varāhasya | (su.ra. 1206)2. mahādevaḥdevairdugdhapayodhirodhasi urā kairnāma manthācalakṣobhaprodgatacandramaḥprabhṛtaye na preṣitāḥ pāṇayaḥ |svīcakre parameka eva bhagavānudvignalokatrayīrakṣāyai kaṭukālakūṭagaralagrāsaṃ sa gaurīśvaraḥ ||1646||vāsudevasenasya |chinne brahmaśiro yadi prathayati preteṣu sakhyaṃ yadikṣīvaḥ krīḍati mātṛbhiryadi ratiṃ dhatte śmaśāne yadi |sṛṣṭvā saṃharati prajā yadi tadāpyādhāya bhaktyā manastaṃ seve karavāṇi kiṃ trijagatī śūnyā sa eveśvaraḥ ||1647||umāpatidharasya |svaṃ cetsaṃcarase vṛṣeṇa laghutā kā nāma digdantināṃvyālaiḥ kaṅkaṇakuṇḍalāni kuruṣe hānirna hemnāmapi |mūrdhanyaṃ tanuṣe jaḍāṃśumayaśaḥ kiṃ nāma lokatrayīdīpasyāmbujabāndhavasya jagatāmīśo'si kiṃ brūmahe ||1648||śailasarvasya |āhāro garalaṃ tṛtīyamalike cakṣuḥ kapālaṃ karevāsaḥ kuñjaracarma bhasmani ratirbhūṣā bhujaṅgādhipaḥ |janmālakṣyamasākṣikaṃ kulamavijñātā ca jātiḥkathaṃ sevyo'smābhirasau piśācapariṣadbhartā hatāḥ smo vayam ||1649||dharmayogeśvarasya |pāṇau brahmakapālamaśitbhiralaṅkāro'ṅgarāgaścitābhasmāvyāhatamuttarīyamuragaḥ krīḍā samaṃ mātṛbhiḥ |yasyaitānyasamañjasāni tamanācāraiḥ piśācairvṛtaṃkaḥ sthāṇuḥ phalavāñchayā vada vṛṣādanyo janaḥ sevate ||1650||tasyaiva |3. gaṇāḥtulyaiveśvarasevā karma na vidmaḥ purākṛtaṃ kīdṛka|bhṛṅgī yadasthiśeṣo bhṛśataramakṛśaśca kūṣmāṇḍaḥ ||1651||vākpateḥ |eko giriśaḥ svāmī gaṇatā tulyaiva vallabhatvaṃ ca |kiṃ kurmaḥ karmagatau śuṣyati bhṛṅgī vināyakaḥ pīnaḥ ||1652||kasyacita|kapardī bhūtisaṃpanno jagatīpatiradvayaḥ |dhigdaivamavyayaḥ so'pi bhṛṅgī śuṣyatyato bhṛśam ||1653||amoghasya |skande mandāvadhānaṃ carati gaṇapatau maulipātaṃ na dhattevṛnde vṛndārakāṇāṃ vinayavati bhṛśaṃ nādarānātanoti |kiṃ bhūmnā yaśca devīṃ na namati girijāṃ tasya nirvyājavṛtteḥkṣīāsyāpyekaniṣṭhā jayati bhagavatī bhṛṅgiṇastasya bhaktiḥ ||1654||umāpatidharasya |kūṭasthaṃ śravaṇopakaṇṭhavilasatkrūradvijihvāśrayaṃdakṣadveṣiṇamaṅghralaṅghitavṛṣaṃ vaiṣamyabhīmekṣaṇam |īśaṃ nirguṇavyayaprakṛtikaṃ saṃsevya bhṛṅgī cirādyajjīvatyatidurbalena vapuṣā manye sa evotsavaḥ ||1655||kasyacita|4. sūryaḥkiṃ naiva santi subahūni mahāmahāṃsicandro'pyalaṃ bhuvanamaṇḍalamaṇḍanāya |sūryādṛte na tadudeti na cāstametiyenoditena dinamastamitena rātriḥ ||1656||ānandavardhanasya | (su.ra. 1202, kasyacit)rātrāvoṣadhayo jvalanti kalayantyaujjvalyamapyagnayojyotsnāścandramasi sphuranti dadhati jyotīṃṣi tejasvitām |anyacca krimayo'pi bibhrati maholeśānamuṣyaiva tāḥsarvā eva nidhestviṣāṃ bhagavato dīptipraticchāyikāḥ ||1657||umāpatidharasya |asyāmoṣadhayo jvalantu dadhatu jyotīṃṣi kīṭā apipronmīlantu bhujaṅgamaulimaṇayaḥ krīḍantu dīpāṅkurāḥ |praṣṭavyāḥ khalu yūyameva yadi ko'pyastaṃ gate bhāsvatiprauḍaḥadhvāntapayodhimagnajagatī hastāvalambakṣamaḥ ||1658||jalacandrasya |asminnaktamaharvivekavikale kālādhame nīradaiḥsaṃnaddhairabhito niruddhagaganābhogāsu digbhittiṣu |bhānorna prasarantu nāma kiraṇāḥ kiṃ tvasya tejasvinaḥsattāmātraparigraheṇa vikasantyadyāpi padmākarāḥ ||1659||vāsudevasya |jagannetraśreṇītimiraharasiddhāñjanasakhāmayūkhā yasyaite tribhuvanamamoghaṃ vidadhati |aye karmālaṅghyaṃ kalaya kimapīdaṃ tanubhṛtāmulūkānāmandhaṃkaraṇakiraṇaḥ so'baramaṇiḥ ||1660||5. candraḥsudhāṃśorjāteyaṃ kathamapi kalaṅkasya kaṇikāvidhāturdoṣo'yaṃ na ca guṇanidhestasya kimapi |sa kiṃ nātreḥ putro na kimu haracūḍārcanamaṇirna vā hanti dhvāntaṃ jagadupari kiṃ vā na vasati ||1661||daṅkasya |asminnabhyudite jagattrayadiśāmullāsahetau diśāṃāsyamlānihare sudhārasanidhau deve niśāsvāmini |vaktraṃ mudritamambujanma bhavatā cetkiṃ tataḥ śāśvataṃnaitasyeśvaramaulimaṇḍanamaṇergāyanti viśve yaśaḥ ||1662||vaidyagadādharasya |ajani bhagavānasmādvedhāḥ śiraḥsu sudhābhujāṃkṛtapadamidaṃ paṅkapatitagajaḥdūrādeva karañjasarjasaralaprāyānvtlokya drumānkṣutkṣāmo vikalaḥ karī kṣitibhṛtaḥ pādāntike prasthitaḥ |mohādāgata eva nirbharadarīdurge nirālambanonirmagnaḥ kimayaṃ karoti yena kṣaṇānmagnaḥ kāsarakelipaṅkilataṭopānte sa dantābalaḥ ||1847||śālūkasya |raṭitamanucitaṃ te kaḥ karāsphālakālaḥpracalitamatimātraṃ gātranirmajjanāya |kathamapi patitastvaṃ dustare paṅkarāśaukuru karivara dhairyaṃ durjayā daivarītiḥ ||1848||pāmpākasya |kareṇurnāhūtā nijakavalabhāgapraṇayinīna cāmṛṣṭaḥ snehātkarakisalayenāpi kalabhaḥ |sa yenāsau |tvallobhānnanu hastini svayamidaṃ bandhāya dattaṃ vapustvaṃ dūre dhriyase luṭhanti ca śiraḥpīṭhe kaṭhorāṅkuśāḥ ||1853||tasyaiva |no manye dṛḍhabandhanakṣatamidaṃ cakravākaḥtīrāttīramupaiti rauti karuṇaṃ cintāṃ samālambatekāntāṃ dhyāyati niścalena manasā yogīva yuktekṣaṇaḥ |svaccāyāmavalokya kūjati punaḥ kānteti hṛṣṭaḥ khagodhanyāste khalu ye |pakṣāvutkṣipati kṣitau nipatati kroḍe nakhairullikhatyudbāṣpeṇa ca cakṣuṣā sahacaraṃ dhyātvā muhurvīkṣate |cakrāhvā divasāvasānasamaye tattatkarotyākulāyenālohitamaṇḍalo'pi kṛpayā yātyeṣa nāstaṃ raviḥ ||2073||sāhasāṅkasya || (Sv1921)ekenārkaṃ hutavahaśikhāpāṭalenāstasaṃsthaṃpaśyatyakṣṇā sajalalulitenāpareṇa svakāntam |ahnaśchede dayitavirahā śaṅkinī cakravākīdvau saṃkīrṇau racayati kamapi bhavabhūtirvitanute ||2130||kasyacita| (su.ra. 1698)27. pratyekakaviḥvikacakumudakrīḍakrīḍanmadhuvratajhāṅkṛtīrmadakalakuhūkaṇṭhotkaṇṭhāvipañcitapañcamām |abhinavavadhūpremālāpādapi pariṇatairarthavacasormataṃ cedasmākaṃ kaviramarasiṃho vijayate ||2132||śālikanāthasya | (su.ra. 1724)pātu karṇarasāyanaṃ racayituṃ vācaḥ satāṃ saṃmatāvyutpattiṃ paramāmavāptumavadhiṃ labdhuṃ rasasrotasaḥ |bhoktuṃ svādu phalaṃ ca jīvitataroryadyasti te kautukaṃtadbhrātaḥ śṛṇu rājaśekharakaveḥ sūktīḥ sudhāsyandanīḥ ||2133||śaṅkaravarmaṇaḥ | (bā.rā. 1.17, vi.śā.bha. 1.17, su.ra. 1700)dhigdhiktānsamayānpariśramarujo vaktuṃ giro nīrasāyatrāmūrnipatanti vallaṇaguṇotkhātāmṛtaprītayaḥ |romṇāṃ nṛtyabhuvo vilocanapayaḥpūrābdhicandrodayāḥsāhityapratigaṇḍagarvagalanaṃ glānikriyāhetavaḥ ||2134||vallaṇasya | (su.ra. 1703)devīṃ vācamupāsate hi bahavaḥ sāraṃ tu sārasvataṃjānīte nitarāmasau gurukulakliṣṭo murāriḥ kaviḥ |ābdharlaṅghita eva vānarabhaṭaiḥ kiṃ tvasya gambhīrtāmāpātālanimagnapīvaratanurjānāti manthācalaḥ ||2135||murāreḥ | (Kuval, p. 58; su.ra. 1701)28. manasvikaviḥvinyastā vikacaprasūnaghaṭanācāryeṇa kaṇṭhocitāmāleyaṃ bhujagabhrameṇa bhavatā janmāndha kiṃ dhūyate |etasyāḥ kṣatirastu nāma kiyatī saṃvītahāsodgamāstvāmanyonyakarārpaṇapraṇayinaḥ paśyanti viśve janāḥ ||2136||jalacandrasya |avadhehi kṣaṇamehi bhrātarbhāvajña bhāvaya giraṃ naḥ |carame cakāsti cetasi mūkasvapnopamo bhāvaḥ ||2137||gosokasya |stambhāvadhehi nimiṣaṃ paṭhāmi sūktīḥ svacittanirvṛttaye |mā budhyasva na tāvadvāgulkābhiḥ kadarthayasi ||2138||vallaṇasya |śrīmadbhirdraviṇavyayavyatikarakleśādavajñāyasedveṣānbhaḥparipūrṇakarṇakuharairnākarṇyase sūribhiḥ |itthaṃ vyarthitavāñchiteṣu hi mudhaivāsmāsu kiṃ khidyasemātaḥ kāvyasudhe kathaṃ kva bhavatīmunmudrayāmo vayam ||2139||tasyaiva |arvācīnavacaḥ prapañcasukhināṃ duḥśikṣitānāṃ purogambhīraṃ kavipuṅgavasya kimaho sarvasvamuddhāṭyate |vyarthaṃ kardamagandhagauravahṛtagrāmīṇagoṣṭhīmukheko'yaṃ nāma sacetano'sti ya iha prastauti kastūrikām ||2140||tasyaiva |29. kavidānaṃniṣpanne sati candracūḍacarite tattannṛpaprakriyājātaiḥ sārdhamarātirājakaśiroratnāñjalīnāṃ trayam |saptasvarṇaśatāni viṃśatiśatīrūpyasya lakṣatrayaṃgrāmāṇāṃ śatamantaraṅgakavaye cāṇakyacandro dadau ||2141||umāpatidharasya |dantivyūhaṃ kanakakalitaṃ cāmare hemadaṇḍaṃyo gauḍendrādalabhata kavikṣmābhṛtāṃ cakravartī |khyāto yaśca śrutidharatayā vikramādityagoṣṭhīvidyābhartuḥ khalu vararucerāsasāda pratiṣṭhām ||2142||dhoyīkasya |kanakakunḍalamaṇḍitabhāṣiṇeśakaripurviṣayāndaśa vidviṣaḥ |magadhakekayakeralakośalānkariśataṃ ca madālasalocanam ||2143||amaroḥ |amuṣmai caurāya pratinihatamṛtyupratibhiyeprabhuḥ prītaḥ prādāduparitanapādadvayakṛte |suvarṇānāṃ koṭīrdaśa daśanakoṭikṣatagirīngajendrānapyaṣṭau madamuditakūjanmadhulihaḥ ||2144||tasyaiva |śloko'yaṃ hariṣābhidhānakavinā devasya tasyāgratoyāvadyāvadudīritaḥ śakavadhūvaidhavyadīkṣāguroḥ |tāvattāvadupoḍhasāndrapulakastasmai sa devo dadaulakṣaṃ lakṣamakhaṇḍitaṃ madhukaravyālolagaṇḍaṃ gajam ||2145||tasyaiva |30. guṇigarvaḥṣaṭtarkānapi śabdaśāsanamapi sthānaiḥ sthitaṃ pañcabhirmīmāṃsādvayamapyananyasadṛśīṃ sāhityavidyāmapi |vidmaḥ kiṃ ca mahāvikalpabahalajvālāvalītāpiteṣvāsmākeṣu na jalpavahniṣu punaḥ kaiḥ kaiḥ pataṅgāyitam ||2146||tapasvinaḥ |tāvattārkikacakravartipadavī tāvatkavīnāṃ girastāvaccāpratimallatāmadabharaḥ sāhityapāṇḍityayoḥ |yāvanna pratiparvanirbharasudhānirvājabījaṃ kṣaṇādvāgvallyo vilasanti karṇakuhare śrīdevabodheritāḥ ||2147||devabodhasya |bindudvandvaraṅgitāgrasaraṇiḥ kartā śirobindukaṃkarmetyanvayakalpanāṃ vidadhate ye ke'pi tebhyo namaḥ |ye tu granthasahasraśāṇakaṣaṇatruṭyatkalaṅgairgirāmullāsaiḥ kavayanti vallaṇakavisteṣveva saṃnahyate ||2148||vallaṇasya |yathā yūnastadvatparamaramaṇīyāpi ramaṇīkumārāṇāmantaḥkaraṇaharaṇaṃ kaiva kurute |maduktiścedantarmadayati sudhībhūya sudhiyaḥkimasyā nāma syādarasapuruṣānādarabharaiḥ ||2149||kavipaṇḍitaśrīharṣasya | (ṇc22.152)sarvasvaṃ gṛhavartikuntalapatirgṛhṇātu tanme punarbhāṇḍāgāramakhaṇḍameva hṛdaye jāgarti sārasvatam |bhoḥ kṣudrāstyajata pramodamacirādeṣyanti manmandiraṃhelāndolitakarṇatālakaraṭiskandhādhirūḍhāḥ śriyaḥ ||2150||silhaṇasya |31. vāṇīsuvarṇālaṅkārā prakaṭitarasāśleṣanipuṇāsphuradvaidarbhoktirlalitapadabandhakramagatiḥ |lasadbhūyo bhāvā mṛdurapi vimardocitatanuḥkavīndra tvadvāṇī harati hariṇākṣīva hṛdayam ||2151||sākokasya | (su.ra. 1716)ghanarasamayī gabhīrā vakrimasubhagopajīvitā kavibhiḥ |avagāḍhā ca punīte gaṅgā baṅgālavāṇī ca ||2152||baṅgālasya |vāṇi vraja suralokaṃ triśaraṇapālo'pi devi tatraiva |saṃprati kāvyapariśramavadhirairavadhīraṇāṃ yāsi ||2153||tripurāripālasya |pipāsuḥ pīyūṣaṃ tvamasi sarasasvādumadhuraṃśrutibhyāmaśrāntaḥ piba madhuramṛdvīḥ kavigiraḥ |athaitāḥ santoṣaṃ vidadhati na ceccetasi tataḥsudhāpi syānmanye pṛthuvamathulābhāya bhavataḥ ||2154||dhañjokasya |iyaṃ gauruddāmā tava nibiḍabandhāpi hi kathaṃna vaidarbhādanyatspṛśati sulabhatve'pi hi katham |avandhyā ca khyātā bhuvi kathamagamyā kavivṛṣaiḥkathaṃ vā pīyūṣaṃ sravati bahu dugdhāpi bahubhiḥ ||2155||śabdārṇavasya | (su.ra. 1725)32. kāvyamyadetadvāgarthavyatikaramayaṃ kiñcidamṛtaṃtadānandasyandaiḥ sahṛdayamanāṃsi snapayati |idaṃ kāvyaṃ tattvaṃ sphurati tu yadatrānuparamaṃtadantarbuddhīnāṃ sphuṭamatha ca vācāmaviṣayaḥ ||2156||hṛṣīkeśasya (su.ra. 1715, sū.mu. 4.34)kavalayati na cetastasya dāridryaduḥkhaṃna ca piśunajanoktiḥ karṇakaṇḍūṃ karoti |varakavikṛtagoṣṭhībandhagandhopabhogeya iha madhu vamantīṃ kāvyacintāṃ karoti ||2157||vyāḍeḥ |etatkavīndramukhacandramasaḥ kadācitkāvyābhidhānamamṛtaṃ yadi nāgāliṣyata|saṃsāriṇāṃ vividhaduḥkhasahasrabhājāṃcetovinodasadanaṃ kimihābhaviṣyata||2158||surabheḥ |te varṇāḥ sapadakramāstadabhidhāvaidagdhyamavyāhṛtaṃgumphaḥ ko'pi sapaktrimaḥ sahṛdayāsvādyo rasaḥ ko'pyasau |he sabhyāḥ paribhāvya mādṛśakṛtīrbrūta kvacinniṣkṛtaṃkiṃ tatrāstyaparaṃ purātanakaveryenaiṣa kolāhalaḥ ||2159||gosokasya |anudghuṣṭaḥ śabdairatha ca ghaṭanātprasphuṭarasaḥpadānāmarthātmā ramayati natūttānitarasaḥ |yathā kiṃciddṛśyaḥ pavanacalacīnāṃśukatayāstanābhogaḥ strīṇāṃ harati na tathonmudritavapuḥ ||2160||dharmāśokasya | (su.ra. 1705)33. kāvyamātsaryamvāyūdgāragatistataḥ pariṇatiḥ sṛṣṭeraho kauśalaṃvāyuḥ śloka ihaiva santi sakalāḥ kāvyasya te te guṇāḥ |kasyāyaṃ mama huṃ tathaiva śṛṇumaḥ samyakpunaḥ paṭhyatāṃjānāmi sphuṭatātra nāsti bhaṇitaṃ cānyaiḥ purāṇaṃ paṭha ||2161||kasyacita|drākṣāpākaviḍambinīmapi giraṃ mātsaryadāhajvarānnācāmanti manāgarocakaparādhīnāḥ kiyanto janāḥ |ākaṇṭhaṃ paripīya satkavigavīpīyūṣamanye punarno mādyanti yaśaḥśarīrapiśitatrāsāya baddhaspṛhāḥ ||2162||jalacandrasya |bhrāmyanti kutukāvalambitamanāḥ sārakhatānāśramānasmai vāṇi vidhehi durjanamarusthānāya dūre namaḥ |na prāṇanti yadarpaṇādiha guṇāḥ kāmaṃ yaśovallayaḥkhidyante sarasāpi satkavirasasrotasvatī sīdati ||2163||tasyaiva |kva hāsaleśaḥsvābodhādaprasādadhvananamasadavadyoktihelāvahelā |maunavyāsaṅgavārtāntarapararuciraślokapāṭhādayastesoḍhavyāḥ ke kiyantaḥ śiva śiva kavi te kucchalā matsarāṇām ||2165||kavipaṇḍitaśrīharṣasya ||34. kāvyacauraḥdhanyāste bhuvanaṃ punanti kavayo yeṣāmajasraṃ gavāmuddāmadhvanipallavena paritaḥ pūtā diśāṃ bhittayaḥ |dhiktānniḥsvavilāsinaḥ kavikhalāṃllokadvayadrohiṇonityākampitacetasaḥ paragavīdohena jīvanti ye ||2166||jalacandrasya |baddho lambitacūḍamañjalirayaṃ vāṇi kṣamasvāmṛtaṃna brūmastvayi devabhāvasulabhaṃ na dyotate tanmahaḥ |syāccedīṣadapi prasahya rasanāṭaṅkaiḥ kathaṃ khaṇḍaśaśchindanto bhavatīṃ kavīndraghaṭitāṃ jīvantyamī dasyavaḥ ||2167||vaidyagadādharasya |niḥśaṅkaṃ hara kāñcanānyanibhṛtaṃ dārānguroḥ śīlayasvacchandaṃ piba vāruṇīṃ jahi nirātaṅkaṃ dvijānāṃ kulam |taistaiḥ pātakibhiḥ samaṃ vasa sukhaṃ mā satkavīnāṃ kṛthāḥsteyaṃ sūktinidhānasadmani durucchedaṃ hi tatkilbiṣam ||2168||tasyaiva |iyaṃ gaurekā naḥ kvacidapi na saṃyojanavidhāvamuṣyāḥ paśyāmo rasabharamucaḥ kāṃcidaparām |gale baddhā dadhmo yadi na dhṛitiruddāmavidhṛtaubhayaṃ gocorebhyastadiha ka upāyaḥ prabhavatu ||2169||selhūkasya |hṛtkaṇṭhaśrutibhūṣaṇāni bahuśo bhrātaḥ suvarṇānyapisvānyasmābhirupāhṛtāni vipaṇisthāneṣu dainyānna kim |dhikkarmāṇi tulaiva nāsti na kaṣagrāvā na mānakramona kretā na parīkṣakaḥ paramabhūduccairbhayaṃ durjanāna||2170||jitāreḥ |35. sajjanaḥañjalisthāni puṣpāṇi vāsayanti karadvayam |aho sumanasāṃ vṛttirvāmadakṣiṇayoḥ samā ||2171||gobhaṭasya | (su.ra. 1232, śā.pa. 199)ayaṃ nijaḥ paro veti gaṇanā laghucetasām |udāracaritānāṃ tu vasudhaiva kuṭumbakam ||2172||keśaṭasya | (su.ra. 1241)sujano na yāti vairaṃ parahitabuddhirvināśakāle'pi |chede'pi candanataruḥ surabhayati mukhaṃ kuṭhārasya ||2173||śrīvyāsapādānām | (Sv241, śā.pa. 237, sū.mu. 6.12)asanto nābhyarthyāḥ suhṛdapi na yācyastanudhanaḥpriyāvṛttirnyāyyā caritamasubhaṅge'pyamalinam |vipadyuccaiḥ stheyaṃ padamanuvidheyaṃ ca mahatāṃsatāṃ kenoddiṣṭaṃ viṣamamasidhārāvratamidam ||2174||dharmakīrteḥ | (su.ra. 1213, Sv280)ye dīneṣu dayālavaḥ spṛśati yānalpo'pi na śrīmadovyagrā sū.mu. 6.30)36. durjanaḥete snehamayā iti mā mā kṣudreṣu yāta viśvāsam |siddhārthānāmeṣāṃ sneho'pyaśrūṇi pātayati ||2176||gobhaṭasya | (su.ra. 1296)ko'rthānprāpya na garvito bhuvi naraḥ kasyāpadostaṃ gatāḥstrībhiḥ kasya na khaṇḍitaṃ bhuvi manaḥ ko nāma rājñāṃ priyaḥ |kaḥ kālasya na gocarāntaragataḥ ko'rtho gato gauravaṃko vā durjanavāgurāsu patitaḥ kṣemeṇa yātaḥ pumāna||2177||kasyacita| (Sv3470, śā.pa. 1534)dūrāducchritapāṇirārdranayanaḥ protsāritārdhāsanogāḍhāliṅganatatparaḥ priyakathāpraśneṣu dattottaraḥ |antargūḍhaviṣo bahirmadhumayaścātīva māyāpaṭuḥko nāmāyamapūrvanāṭakavidhiryaḥ śikṣito durjanaiḥ ||2178||binduśarmaṇaḥ | (Sv342)guṇotkarṣadveṣātprakṛtimahatāmapyasadṛśaṃkhalaḥ kiṃcidvākyaṃ racayati ca vistārayati ca |na cedeṣāṃ satatadurgataḥ sajjanonṛpāṅgaṇagataḥ khalo manasi sapta śalyāni me ||2180||śilhaṇasya | (ṇs10, Sv3458, sā.da. 10.110, śā.pa. 1530)37. sujanadurjanaujīvantu sādhutaravaḥ sukṛtāmbusiktānaśyantu paṅkapatitāḥ khalapāṃśavo'pi |ye dhārayantyanugatopakṛtivratāniyaiḥ sannidhau paraguṇā malinīkriyante ||2181||saṅketasya |satsaṅgādbhavati hi sādhutā khalānāṃsādhūnāṃ na tu cettattvamanayostadā stokaṃ brūmaḥ paricinu vacastvaṃ sadasatoḥ |satāṃ svāntaṃ yattanmadhumadhuramantaḥ kaṭu bahirbahiḥ svādu svacchaṃ viṣaviṣamamantastadasatām ||2184||jiyokasya |ārambhagurvī |viṣayapatiralubdho dhenubhirdhāma pūtaṃkaticidabhimatāyāṃ sīmni sīrā vahanti |śithilayati ca bhāryā nātitheyīṃ saparyāmiti sukṛtamanena vyañjitaṃ naḥ phalena ||2187||śubhāṅkasya |dhārānipātaravabodhitapañjarasthadātyūhaḍambarakarambitakaṇṭhakūjāḥ |aṭṭeṣu kāṇḍapaṭavāritaśīkareṣudhanyāḥ pibanti mukhatāmarasaṃ vadhūnām ||2188||śrīhanūmataḥ | (su.ra. 224)śilāpaṭṭodghṛṣṭā (su.ra. 1621)39. udāttaḥvimalamatibhiḥ kairapyetajjagajjanitaṃ purāvidhṛtamaparairdattaṃ cānyairvijitya tṛṇaṃ yathā |iha hi bhuvanānyanye dhīrāścaturdaśa bhuñjatekatipayapurasvānte puṃsāṃ ka eṣa madajvaraḥ ||2191||bhartṛhareḥ | (Ss2.14)kenenduḥ kumudeṣu kena taraṇiḥ padmeṣu kenāmbudaḥsāraṅgeṣvatha kena śākhiṣu madhurdākṣiṇyamadhyāpitaḥ |tattuṅgānanubhūtasaurabhaparīvāropakāraṃ ||2210||kasyacita| (Sv3232)43. manasvisevakaḥsoḍhaṃ dvāḥsthitaduḥsthitadurvacaḥ kaṭu tato dṛṣṭo durīśaścirādudgīrṇāḥ svaguṇāśca yācitamatha śrotre kṛtā neti gīḥ |asminpātakapañcake sati sthīyate ||taraṇikasya |keśāḥ kāśanibhāḥ kapālaphalake tvagbhistaraṅgāyitaṃkācenocitatārakeṇa khacite paryaśruṇī locane |aṅgānāmavasāditāpi ca girāṃ kampastathāpyeṣa memohaḥ snehamayo na bhavatyai ||2254||dharmapālasya |digvibhramaṃ daśanakhaṇḍanamaṅgabhaṅgaṃkeśagrahaṃ ratividhau madanādaraṃ ca |śvāsaprakampajaḍabhāvasughūrṇitānidhatte jarā praṇayinīva mayopagūḍhā ||2255||kasyacita|52. vṛddhaḥsvasti sukhebhyaḥ saṃprati salilāñjalireṣa manmathakathāyāḥ |tā api māmativayasaṃ taraladṛśaḥ saralamīkṣante ||2256||śatānandasya | (Sv3395, su.ra. 1522)ākrāntaṃ valibhiḥ prasahya palitairatyantamāskanditaṃvārdhakyaṃ ślathasaṃdhibandhanatayā niḥsthāma nirdhāma ca |etanme ||2258||kasyacita|sthūlaprāvaraṇo'tivṛttakathanaḥ kāsāśrulālāvilobhugnāṅghritrikapṛṣṭhajānujaghano mugdho'tithīnvārayana|śṛṇvandhṛṣṭavadhūvacāṃsi dhanuṣā duḥsahaśītavātatapanakleśā na taptaṃ tapaḥ |dhyātaṃ vittamaharniśaṃ na ca punarviṣṇoḥ padaṃ śāśvataṃtattatkarma kṛtaṃ yadeva munibhistaistaiḥ phalairvañcitam ||2261||bhartṛhareḥ | (Ss1.9ḥ Sv3178, śā.pa. 4153, su.ra. 1632)nāthe śrīpuruṣottame trijagatāmekādhipe cetasāsevye svasya padasya dātari sure nārāyaṇe tiṣṭhati |yaṃ kaṃcitpuruṣādhamaṃ katipayagrāmeśamalpārthadaṃsevāyai mṛgayāmahe naramaho mūḍhā varākā vayam ||2262||tasyaiva | (Ss1.11)uṣasyeva bhrāntaṃ hatajaṭharahetostata itaḥsvayaṃ ca svaṃ bibhradvicarati kuṭumbaṃ diśi diśi |batāsmābhiḥ kākairiva kavalamātraikamuditairna cāyurdurgatyoravadhiriha labdhaḥ kathamapi ||2263||veśokasya |kauśalyā nanu rodhanā janakabhūrdūrīkṛtā kiṃ tu naprāptā pañcavaṭī na vānarapaterāsāditaṃ sauhṛdam |sāmarṣeṇa na vārirāśiracirādullaṅghitaḥ kevalaṃkākutsthena mayā daśānanatiraskārāspadībhūyate ||2264||hareḥ |janasthāne bhrāntaṃ kanakamṛgatṛṣṇāndhitadhiyāvaco vaidehīti pratipadamudaśru nirvedaḥpitrornopakṛtaṃ himāṃśudhavalaṃ nopārjitaṃ vā yaśomitrāṇāmupakāritā na vihitā dattaṃ na ca svecchayā |gāḍhāliṅganalālasāpi dayitā nāliṅgitā kevalaṃkālo'bhyeti calaṃ ca jīvitamiti kṣuṇṇaṃ |no vā vāmavilocanāmalamukhāmbhojeṣu bhṛṅgāyitaṃmātuḥ kevalameva yauvanavanacchede kuṭhārāyitam ||2269||bhartṛhareḥ | (su.ra. 1498)nākrāntāmbudhimekhalā vasumatī lakṣmīḥ samāveśitāno hṛdayaṃ pūjitā yauvanaśrīḥ |saṃpratyantarnihitasadasadbhāvalabdhaprabodhapratyāhārāpahṛtahṛdayo vartate ko'pi bhāvaḥ ||2311||kasyacita| (Ss4.16)iyaṃ bālā māṃ 1620)yadāsīdajñānaṃ smaratimirasaṃskārajanitaṃtadā dṛṣṭaṃ nārīmayamidamaśeṣaṃ jagadapi |idānīmasmākaṃ paṭutaravivekāñjanajuṣāṃsamībhūtā dṛṣṭistribhuvanamapi brahma manute ||2313||kasyacita| (Ss4.14, sa.ka.ā. 5.115; su.ra. 1611)kimasmānvāmākṣi smaravijayayātrābhyudayikairvṛthā śāntānlājjairiva hasitaleśaiḥ snapayasi |idānīṃ golomnā śucini tanukālāvujaṭharepatadbhaikṣyāhāre valati hi paraṃ lāñchini manaḥ ||2314||jalokasya |gataḥ kālo yatra praṇayini mayi premakuṭilaḥkaṭākṣaḥ kālindīlaghulaharivṛttiḥ prabhavati |idānīmasmākaṃ jaraṭhakamaṭhīpṛṣṭhakaṭhināmonovṛttistatkiṃ vyasanini mudhaiva kṣapayasi ||2315||vallaṇasya | (Ss4.13, sū.mu. 131.33, su.ra. 1599)64. niḥspṛhaḥvāso valkalamāstaraḥ kisalayānyokastarūṇāṃ talaṃmūlāni kṣataye kṣudhāṃ girinadītoyaṃ tṛṣāśāntaye |krīḍā mugdhamṛgairvayāṃsi suhṛdo naktaṃ pradīpaḥ śaśīsvādhīne'pi dhane tathāpi kṛpaṇā yācanta ityadbhutam ||2316||kasyacita| (su.ra. 1598, Ss2.20)nītāḥ puṇyāgnigehe śiśirarajanayaḥ ||2317||yogeśvarasya |nijaṃ karma kṣīṇaṃ sa khalu viparīto hatavidhiḥsukṛtye vā tattve bhṛśamupagatā yatnanicayāḥ |idānīmasmākaṃ sphuradurujarājarjaramidaṃvapurjātaṃ tṛṣṇe virama daridraḥ ||2319||kṛṣṇamiśrasya | (Sv3475, śā.pa. 308, da.rū.. under4.2, Vai' 177)mātarlakṣmi bhajasva kaṃcidaparaṃ matkāṅkṣiṇāṃ mā sma bhūrbhogebhyaḥ spṛhayālavastava vaśāḥ kā niḥspṛhāṇāmasi |sadyaḥsyūtapalāśapatrapuṭikāpātre pavitrīkṛtairbhikṣāsaktubhireva samprati vayaṃ kāśyāṃ samīhāmahe ||2320||lakṣmīdharasya | (Ss4.11, su.ra. 1612)65. vanagamanotsukaḥaye diṣṭyā naṣṭo mama gṛhapiśācīparicayaḥparāvṛttaṃ mohātsphurati ca manāgbrahmaṇi manaḥ |vikāro'pyakṣāṇāṃ galita iva nirbhāti viṣayāttathāpi kṣetrajñaḥ spṛhayati vanāya pratimuhuḥ ||2321||bhartṛhareḥ |ramyaṃ ||2322||vijñātātmanaḥ | (Ss2.15, Sv3326, śā.pa. 4114, sū.mu. 131.51)āstāmakaṇṭhakamidaṃ vasudhādhipatyaṃtrailokyarājyamapi deva tṛṇāya manye |niḥśaṅkasuptahariṇīkulasaṅkulāsucetaḥ paraṃ luṭhati śailavanasthalīṣu ||2323||śālavāhasya | (su.ra. 1606, Ss2.16)hariṇacaraṇakṣuṇṇopāntāḥ saśādvalanirjharāḥkusumaśavalairviṣvagvātaistaraṅgitapādapāḥ |muditavihagaśreṇīcitradhvanipratināditāmanasi na mudaṃ kasyādadhyuḥ śivā vanabhūtayaḥ ||2324||guṇākarabhadrasya | (su.ra. 1595, Ss2.17)kuraṅgāḥ kalyāṇaṃ prativiṭapamārogyamaṭavisravanti kṣemaṃ te pulinakuśalaṃ bhadramupalāḥ |niśāntādasvantātkathamapi ca niṣkāntamadhunāmano'smākaṃ dīrghāmabhilaṣati yuṣmatparicitim ||2325||lakṣmīdharasya | (su.ra. 1626, Ss2.19)66. tapovanampratyagragomayaviliptavitardikānipūrṇāhutiprabalavahniśikhāśatāni |śuśrūṣamāṇamṛgalocanakanyakānitānyadya tāpasavanāni mano haranti ||2326||narasiṃhasya |ete nīvāravaprāḥ ||2327||maghoḥ |etāni kratupṛṣṭhavediviluṭhadviprāṇi vātapramīcchannopāntatarūṇi paśya dadhate puṇyāśramāṇi śriyam |yānyutkṣipya manaḥ parāñcati paraṃ nārāyaṇārādhanaśraddhāmoditamekadaiva ||2329||śrīmallakṣmaṇasenasya |śārdūlī snehagarbhaṃ mukulitanayanaṃ leḍhi śāvaṃ hariṇyābandhuprītyā śikhaṇḍī tirayati phaṇināmātapaṃ kīrṇabarhaḥ |siṃhī rakṣatyapatyaṃ svamiva kalabhakaṃ vistīrṇamāśādaśakamapamalaṃ talpamasvalpamurvī |yeṣāṃ niḥsaṅgatāṅgīkaraṇapariṇatisvastisantoṣiṇastedhanyāḥ saṃnyastadainyavyatikaranikarāḥ karma nirmūlayanti ||2331||nagnācāryasya | (Ss4.7)dhigdhiktānkṛminirviśeṣavapuṣaḥ sphūrjanmahāsiddhayoniṣpandīkṛtaśāntayo'pi ca tapaḥkārā gṛheṣvāsane |taṃ vidvāṃsamiha stumaḥ karapuṭībhikṣālpaśāke'pi vābālāvaktrasarojinīmadhuni vā yasyāviśeṣo rasaḥ ||2332||vallaṇasya | (Ss4.10, su.ra. 1609)vārāṃstrīnabhiṣuṇvate vidadhate vanyaiḥ śarīrasthitīraiṇeyyāṃ tvaci saṃviśanti vasate cāpi tvacaṃ tāravīm |tatpaśyanti ca dhāma ||2335||tasyaiva | (Sḥak7.12, sa.ka.ā. 1.106)68. bahuviṣayaśāntiḥnaikaṃ janma tavaiva vatsa na paraṃ tulyā ca karmasthitirbhoktavyeṣu sukheṣu hṛṣyasi mudhā duḥkheṣu kiṃ tāmyasi |bhrātaḥ sthairyamupehi nanviha bhavānsaṃsāradīrghādhvagaḥsucchāyāstaravaḥ kvacinmarubhuvaḥ kvāpi pracaṇḍātapāḥ ||2336||daśarathasya |nanvātmanyavadhīyatāṃ gṛharasādvairāgyamādhīyatāṃcetaḥ samprati damyatāṃ surasarittīre sadā sthīyatām |bhikṣārthaṃ vyavasīyatāṃ samucitaṃ satkarma saṃciyatāṃkṛṣṇaścetasi dhīyatāṃ parataraṃ brahmānusandhīyatām ||2337||bhartṛhareḥ | (Ss3.11)te tāvatkṛtinaḥ ||2338||tasyaiva |vivekaḥ kiṃ so'pi svarasavalitā yatra na kṛpāsa kiṃ yogo yasminbhavati na parānugraharasaḥ |sa kiṃ dharmo yatra sphurati na paradrohaviratiḥśrutaṃ tatkiṃ sākṣādupaśamapadaṃ yanna nayati ||2339||kasyacita| (su.ra. 1629, Ss2.25)kṛmikulacittaṃ lālāklinnaṃ vigandhijugupsitaṃnirupamarasaṃ prītyā khādannarāsthi nirāmiṣam |surapatimapi śvā pārśvasthaṃ vilokya na śaṅkatena hi gaṇayati kṣudro jantuḥ parigrahaphalgutām ||2340||śūrasya (nī.śa. 9 (30); su.ra. 1628, Ss2.9)69. athādhyātmavitbhavāraṇyaṃ bhīmaṃ tanugṛhamidaṃ chidrabahulaṃbalī kālaścauro niyatamasitā moharajanī |gṛhītvā jñānāsiṃ viratiphalakaṃ śīlakavacaṃsamādhānaṃ kṛtvā sthirataradṛśo jāgṛta janāḥ ||2341||silhaṇasya |aye dūrabhrāntaṃ viṣayaviṣamāraṇyavipatheparibhrāntaṃ ceto |nānāpyekaṃ yadiha daharaṃ puṇḍarīkaṃ yadokastoke yasyāpyanubhavavidhau na svadante madhūni |yasyonmeṣāddinamaṇiruco'pyandhakāraprakārāḥśaśvattasmai praṇama hṛdaya brahmaṇe śāśvatāya ||2345||kasyacita|70. bhavitavyatāsṛjati tāvadaśeṣaguṇākaraṃpuruṣaratnamalaṅkaraṇaṃ bhuvaḥ |tadanu tatkṣaṇabhaṅgi karoti cedahaha kaṣṭamapaṇḍitatā vidheḥ ||2346||kasyacita| (Sv3126, śā.pa. 4000, sū.mu. 131.39, su.ra. 1473)adhvaśramāya caraṇau virahāya dārāabhyarthanāya vacanaṃ na vapurjarāyai |etāni me vidadhatastasya sarvadaivadhātastrapā na yadi kiṃ na pariśramo'pi ||2350||kasyacita|71. daivaṃkarotu nāma nītijño vyavasayamitastataḥ |phalaṃ punastadevāsya yadvidhermanasi sthitam ||2351||kasyacita| (sū.mu. 112.10)bhugnāśasya |nṛtyadvetālamālāvalayitavikaṭaprāntamuḍḍāmarograprakrīḍaḍḍākinīkaṃ pratipadamudayatpūtanotphālalīlam |utkhelatkolakelīkavalitavighasagrāsasaṃsaktagṛdhrākṛṣṭannasthipramodaṃ na janayati kathaṃ 1529)cañcatpakṣābhidhātajvalitahutavahaprauḍhadhāmnaścitāyāḥkroḍādvyākṛṣṭamūrterahamahamikayā caṇḍacañcugraheṇa |sadyastaptaṃ śavasya jvaladiva piśitaṃ bhūri jagdhvārdhadagdhaṃpaśyāntaḥ pluṣyamāṇaḥ praviśati salilaṃ satvaraṃ gṛdhravṛddhaḥ ||2365||tasyaiva | (sū.mu. 94.6, su.ra. 1528)74. samasyāthūthūkṛtya vamadbhiradhvagajanairaprāptakaṇṭhaṃ payaḥśuṣyattālugalairviruttya lavaṇodanvānupālabhyate |kena kṣārakhane vṛthaiva bhavato nāmānṛtaṃ nirmitaṃpāthodhirjaladhiḥ payodhirudadhirvārāṃ nidhirvāridhiḥ ||2366||vidyāyāḥ |aye keyaṃ dhanyā dhavalagṛhavātāyanagatātulākoṭikvāṇairviṣamaviśikhaṃ jāgarayati |purā yā prāṇeśe gatavati kṛtā puṣpadhanuṣāśarāsārai rātriṃdivamakṛpamujjāgarakṛśā ||2367||kasyacita| (sū.mu. 49.11)haraśirasi 1726)prāsādāḥ śikharaskhalajjaladharāḥ khātāni vārāṃ nidhispardhāvantyupayānti bhūmisamatāṃ kālena rājñāmapi |kṣudrasyāpi kaveḥ sadartharacanākīrtistu yā vāṅmayīnādṛṣṭvā yugaviplavaṃ punarasau |sadbandhurguṇasindhurandhalaguḍo dharmasya vartmāvaneḥśrīmallakṣmaṇasenadakṣiṇabhujādaṇḍo'pi daṇḍe kaṭuḥ ||2376||dharmādhikaraṇamadhoḥ |yo heloktibhirāhito
